<TR><TD WIDTH="14%" VALIGN="top" height="15">
<font size="2">&nbsp;</font><B><font size="2">ITEM 2.01.</font></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="138%" VALIGN="TOP" colspan="2" height="15">
<font size="2"><b>Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.</b></font></TD>
</TR>
<TR><TD WIDTH="14%" VALIGN="top" height="23">
  </TD>
<TD WIDTH="138%" VALIGN="TOP" colspan="2" height="23">
<p align="justify"><font size="2">On December 21, 2004, American Eagle
Outfitters, Inc. (the &quot;Company&quot;) completed the disposition of its Bluenotes
retail apparel business to a private company controlled by Mr. Michael Gold (the
&quot;Purchaser&quot;),
owner of YM Inc., (Sales), a prominent Canadian retailer.&nbsp; The disposition
had an effective date of December 5, 2004 and was effected pursuant to an Asset Purchase Agreement (the &quot;Agreement&quot;) dated
November 22, 2004, as amended by an Asset Purchase Amending Agreement (the
&quot;Amending Agreement&quot;) dated December 10, 2004.  The
Company expects to receive approximately $21 million to $23 million as consideration for the
sale of certain of its Bluenotes assets, including inventory and property and
equipment.&nbsp; At closing, the Company had received $12 million of
the aforementioned consideration.&nbsp; The remaining cash proceeds will be
received by the Company as the purchased inventory is sold by the Purchaser in the normal course of
business through April 2, 2005.</font></p>
<p align="justify"><font size="2">A copy of the Agreement is attached hereto as
Exhibit 2.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.&nbsp; A copy of the
Amending Agreement is attached hereto as
Exhibit 2.2 and is incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>
<p align="justify"><font size="2">On December 21, 2004, American Eagle
Outfitters, Inc. issued a press release announcing the
completion of the disposition of Bluenotes.&nbsp; A copy of this press release
is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>
  </TD>
</TR>
<TR><TD WIDTH="14%" VALIGN="top" height="8">
  </TD>

<b><u>ASSET PURCHASE AGREEMENT</u></b></p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="center"><b>THIS ASSET PURCHASE AGREEMENT</b>
made the 22<sup>nd</sup> day of November, 2004,</p>
<p class="MsoBodyText" align="center"><b>BETWEEN</b>:</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center"><b>6295215 CANADA INC.</b>,<br>
a corporation existing under the laws of Canada<br>
(the
"<b>Purchaser</b>")</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center">- and -</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center"><b>BLUENOTES LIMITED PARTNERSHIP</b><br>
a limited partnership
formed under the<br>
laws of the Province
of Ontario<br>
(the "<b>Vendor</b>")</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center">- and -</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center"><b>RETAIL LICENSING COMPANY</b><br>
a corporation existing under the laws<br>
of the State of Nevada<br>
(the "<b>Trademark Vendor</b>")</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center">- and -</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center"><b>AMERICAN EAGLE OUTFITTERS<br>
CANADA CORPORATION</b>,<br>
an unlimited liability company existing<br>
under the laws of the Province of Nova Scotia<br>
("<b>American Eagle Canada</b>")</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center">- and -</p>
<p class="centrenb" align="center"><b>3049463 NOVA SCOTIA ULC</b>,<br>
an unlimited liability company existing under<br>
the laws of the Province of Nova Scotia<br>
("<b>GP</b>")</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>WHEREAS</b>
the Vendor carries on business in Canada as a specialty retailer that designs,
markets and sells the Bluenotes/Thriftys brand of clothing and operates
Bluenotes/Thriftys retail stores (the "<b>Purchased Business</b>");</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>&nbsp;AND WHEREAS</b>
all other remaining assets of the Vendor that are used exclusively in connection
with its separate American Eagle clothing division and its National Logistics
Services division (the "<b>Other Divisions</b>") will be retained by the Vendor
and are not subject to the terms of this Agreement;</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>AND WHEREAS GP</b>
is the general partner, and American Eagle Canada is the limited partner, of the
Vendor;</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>AND WHEREAS</b>
American Eagle Canada and GP have agreed to provide certain representations,
warranties and indemnities in favour of the Purchaser relating to the Vendor,
the Trademark Vendor and the Purchased Business and are parties to this
Agreement for such purpose;</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>AND WHEREAS</b>
the Trademark Vendor is the registered and beneficial owner of, among others,
the Bluenotes and Thriftys trademarks and has agreed to sell and assign to the
Purchaser and the Purchaser has agreed to purchase from the Trademark Vendor all
of the Trademark Vendor's right, title and interest in and to such trademarks on
and subject to the terms and conditions contained in this Agreement;</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>AND WHEREAS</b>
the Vendor has agreed to sell to the Purchaser and the Purchaser has agreed to
purchase from the Vendor all of the Vendor's right, title and interest in and to
the assets of the Vendor which relate to the Purchased Business, on and subject
to the terms and conditions contained in this Agreement;</p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><b>THIS AGREEMENT WITNESSES THAT</b>
in consideration of the respective covenants, agreements, representations,
warranties and indemnities of the Parties herein contained and for other good
and valuable consideration (the receipt and sufficiency of which are
acknowledged by each party), the parties agree as follows:</p>
<p class="Article1L1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">

<a name="_Toc88578138">Article 2<br>
PURCHASE AND </a>SALE OF PURCHASED ASSETS</p>

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">

Agreement, the Vendor Group agrees to sell, assign and transfer to the Purchaser
and the Purchaser agrees to purchase from the Vendor Group, on the Closing Date
with effect as of the Effective Time, the undertaking and all of the right,
title and interest of the Vendor Group in and to the property and assets used in
connection with or otherwise relating to the Purchased Business (other than the
Excluded Assets), whether real or personal, tangible or intangible, of every
kind and description and wheresoever situate (collectively, the "<b>Purchased
Assets</b>"), including without limitation, the following assets of the Vendor
Group used in the Purchased Business:</p>

  </blockquote>

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><a name="_Ref87764523">
<b>3.2</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><u><b>Payment of the Purchase Price</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify">The Purchase Price shall be paid and
satisfied by the Vendor in accordance with the following:</p>
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><a name="_Ref88542542">
(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Purchased Trademark Amount<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">.</font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
</p>
  </font>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At the Time of Closing, the Purchaser shall pay the Trademark Vendor the
Purchased Trademark Amount by certified cheque or bank draft payable to or to
the order of the Trademark Vendor.</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88542544">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser shall be entitled to deduct and withhold from the Purchased
Trademark Amount any taxes, charges, deductions or withholdings, now or
hereafter imposed or levied under the Tax Act or the similar law of any province
of Canada, provided that the Purchaser is compelled by law to make such
deductions or withholding and further provided it remits same to the applicable
Governmental Authority in accordance with such Law.</a></p>
  </blockquote>
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87934746">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Purchased Asset Amount</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">.</font></a></p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At the Time of Closing, the Purchaser shall pay to the Vendor the Closing
Date Amount by certified cheque or bank draft payable to or to the order of the
Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87714875">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser covenants that it will make: (i) payments on each Tuesday
of every week during the Payment Term and April 5, 2005 of a portion of the
Purchased Inventory Amount equal to 50% of the Retail Value applicable to the
previous week ending on a Saturday; and (ii) in addition to the last payment in
(i) above on April 5, 2005, a final payment upon the expiry of the Payment Term
equal to the Final Amount, and the Purchaser shall have no right of set-off
against such payments.</a> For these purposes, where
inventory sold has a common SKU, it shall be treated as being sold on a FIFO
basis; </p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At the Time of Closing, the Purchaser shall satisfy a
portion of the Purchased Assets Amount equal to the value of the Assumed
Liabilities by its assumption of the Assumed Liabilities; and </p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
After Closing the following payments shall be made:</p>
    <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L5" align="justify">(A)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
with respect to the working capital adjustment calculated pursuant to
section 3.3, and within the time frame provided for in subsection 3.3(e)
following Closing, if applicable, the Purchaser shall pay the Vendor the amount
referred to in subsection 3.3(e)(i), or the Vendor shall pay the Purchaser the
amount referred to in subsection 3.3(e)(ii), as the case may be; and</p>
<p class="Article1L5" align="justify">(B)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
from time to time following Closing, the adjustments for amounts due to
or from the Vendor from or to landlords in respect of the Leased Stores&nbsp;which
constitute further working capital adjustments, shall be paid by the Vendor to
the Purchaser or by the Purchaser to the Vendor, as the case may be, in
accordance with section 3.4 until all such adjustments have been settled between
the Vendor and the Purchaser.</p>
    </blockquote>
  </blockquote>
</blockquote>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Ref87714627">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>3.3</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Working Capital Adjustment</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87956798">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">(</font></a></font><a name="_Ref87956798"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">a)</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At least three Business Days prior to the Closing Date the Vendor shall
deliver to the Purchaser a statement summarizing its estimate of the Working
Capital Assets and the Working Capital Liabilities and its calculation of the
Estimated Working Capital Amount.</font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"> </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87715149">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
On or before the sixtieth day following the Closing Date, the Vendor
shall calculate the Actual Working Capital Amount and shall deliver to the
Purchaser a statement of the Actual Working Capital Amount (the "<b>Working
Capital Statement</b>").</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88486167">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser shall have a period of thirty days from the date it
receives the Working Capital Statement in which to review the same. If no
objection to the Working Capital Statement is given to the Vendor by the
Purchaser within such thirty day period, the Working Capital Statement shall be
deemed to have been approved as of the last day of such thirty day period.</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87714650">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
If the Purchaser objects to the Working Capital Statement within such
thirty day period by giving notice to the Vendor setting out in reasonable
detail the nature of such objection, the Parties agree to attempt to resolve the
matters in dispute within fifteen days from the date the Purchaser gives such
notice to the Vendor. If all matters in dispute are resolved by the Parties, the
Working Capital Statement shall be modified to the extent required to give
effect to such resolution and shall be deemed to have been approved as of the
date of such resolution. If the Parties cannot resolve all matters in dispute
within such fifteen day period, all unresolved matters shall be submitted to an
independent auditor mutually acceptable to both Parties (the "<b>Arbitrator</b>")
for resolution, and the Arbitrator shall be given access to all materials and
information reasonably requested by it for such purpose. The rules and
procedures to be followed in the arbitration proceedings shall be determined by
the Arbitrator in its discretion. The Arbitrator's determination of all such
matters shall be final and binding on both Parties and shall not be subject to
appeal by either Party. The fees and expenses of the Arbitrator shall be borne
equally by the Vendor and the Purchaser. The Working Capital Statement shall be
modified to the extent required to give effect to the Arbitrator's determination
and shall be deemed to have been approved as of the date of such determination.</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88486211">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Within two Business Days after the Working Capital Statement is deemed to
have been approved in accordance with this section 3.3<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310034003600320037000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->:</a></p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
if the Actual Working Capital Amount exceeds the Estimated Working
Capital Amount, the Purchaser shall pay the Vendor an amount equal to such
excess, together with interest thereon at the Prime Rate from the date following
the Closing Date to but excluding the date of payment, on account of an
adjustment to the Closing Date Amount, and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
if the Actual Working Capital Amount is less than the Estimated Working
Capital Amount, the Vendor shall pay the Purchaser an amount equal to such
excess, together with interest thereon at the Prime Rate from the date following
the Closing Date to but excluding the date of payment on account of an
adjustment to the Closing Date Amount.</p>
  </blockquote>
</blockquote>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Ref88542734">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>3.4</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Subsequent Adjustments</b></u></font></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><u>
</u></p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">Where the Vendor's actual pro rata share
of amounts due to or from it from or to landlords allowed for in the working
capital adjustment in section 3.3<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310034003600320037000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> differs from the estimated amount of such pro rata share of
amounts due to landlords, that difference is payable or receivable, as the case
may be, by the Purchaser and the Vendor, respectively. </p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Toc88578148">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>3.5</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Allocation of Purchase Price</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">The Vendor, the Trademark Vendor and the
Purchaser agree to allocate the Purchase Price among the Purchased Assets and
the Purchased Trademarks in accordance with Schedule 16 and to report the sale
and purchase of the Purchased Assets and the Purchased Trademarks for all
federal, provincial and local tax purposes in a manner consistent with such
allocation.</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Toc88578149">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>3.6</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>ETA Election</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"><font>The Purchaser and the Vendor shall, on
the Closing Date, elect jointly under subsection 167(1) of the ETA and
corresponding provincial legislation, in the form prescribed for the purposes of
that subsection, in respect of the sale and transfer of the Purchased Assets
hereunder. The Purchaser shall file such elections with Canada Revenue Agency or
the appropriate Governmental Authority not later than the last day on which it
is required to file its first return for its reporting period which includes the
Closing Date. </font> </p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Toc88578150">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>3.7</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Transfer Taxes</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The Purchaser shall be liable for all
provincial sales taxes, if any, with respect to the purchase of the Purchased
Assets and the Purchased Trademarks and shall self-assess in respect of such
amounts and remit the same to the applicable Governmental Authority as required
by law.</p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Toc88578151">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>3.8</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"><u><b>Income Tax Election</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72"></font></font>
</font></font></font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Purchaser and the Vendor agree to
elect jointly to have the rules in subsection 20(24) of the Tax Act, and any
equivalent or corresponding provision under applicable provincial or territorial
tax legislation, apply to the obligations of the Vendor in respect of
undertakings which arise from the operation of the Business and to which
paragraph 12(1)(a) of the Tax Act applies. The Purchaser and the Vendor
acknowledge that the Vendor is transferring assets to the Purchaser which have a
value equal to the elected amount as consideration for the assumption by the
Purchaser of such obligations of the Vendor.</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">
<a name="_Toc88578152">Article 4<br>
ASSUMPTION OF LIABILITIES</a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Ref87714663">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>4.1</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Assumption of Certain Liabilities by the
Purchaser</b></u></font></a><font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></p>
</font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">Subject to the provisions of this
Agreement, the Purchaser agrees to assume, pay, satisfy, discharge, perform and
fulfil, from and after the Effective Time, the following obligations and
liabilities of the Vendor in connection with the Purchased Business arising in
the ordinary course after the Effective Time (the "Assumed Liabilities"):</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3">(a)</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Assumed Contracts;</p>
<p class="Article1L3">(b)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
obligations and liabilities respecting the Transferred Employees, subject
to subsection 10.23(c)<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380038003400380030003700320030000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> and subsection 10.23(d)<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380038003400380031003700350032000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->; </p>
<p class="Article1L3">(c)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Inventory On Order Amount; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3">(d)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Working Capital Liabilities.</p>
</blockquote>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="">
<p></font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><a name="_Ref87714849">
<b>4.2</b><font style="">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"><font style="text-decoration: underline">
<u><b>Excluded Liabilities</b></u></font></font></a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">The Parties acknowledge and agree that
the Purchaser is not assuming any liability or obligation of any of the Vendor
Group in relation to the Purchased Business or otherwise except for the Assumed
Liabilities that are expressly and specifically provided for in this Agreement
(the "<b>Excluded Liabilities</b>"). For greater certainty and without limiting
the foregoing, but subject to section 4.1, the Excluded Liabilities include, and
the Purchaser shall not assume any obligation or liability under and shall not
be liable for any Losses in respect of any of the following:</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the operations of the Purchased Business up to the Effective Time;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any liability under a Contract relating to the Purchased Business that is
not an Assumed Contract, including for greater certainty, the lease of the
Excluded Leased Store;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any liabilities under the Assumed Contracts that accrue during or that
are attributable to the period preceding the Effective Time, including without
limitation, any liabilities that relate to a breach by the Vendor of its
obligations thereunder;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any liabilities relating to the Excluded Leased Store, including without
limitation, all operating, sale and maintenance expenses; </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any amounts owing by the Vendor to any supplier or other third party for
Purchased Inventory;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any liabilities relating to the Xerox Lease;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any liabilities in respect of Taxes of the Vendor Group excluding the
real estate tax liabilities of the tenant arising under the Store Leases
relating to the period after the Effective Time;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any liabilities relating to the Purchased Business arising prior to or
relating to the period prior to the Effective Time that have not been disclosed
to the Purchaser in writing; </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(i)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any cause of action relating to the Purchased Business, the Purchased
Assets or the Purchased Trademarks that arises prior to the Effective Time;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(j)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any environmental contamination or pollution arising from the operations
of the Purchased Business or relating to any of the Purchased Assets prior to
the Effective Time;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(k)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the employment of the Employees by the Vendor (subject to the Purchaser's
recognition of Employees' service as recognized by the Vendor pursuant to
subsection 10.23(a)<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380038003500370036003200390030000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->), including without limitation, wages, accrued vacation pay,
employee benefits, Taxes and all other amounts owing to such Employees or
otherwise accruing during or attributable to the period preceding the Effective
Time, notwithstanding any subsequent employment of the Employees by the
Purchaser;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(l)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Excluded Employees and those Employees who do not accept the
Purchaser's offer of employment, including without limitation, any wages,
severance pay, accrued vacation pay, accrued statutory holiday pay, employee
benefits, Taxes and other amounts owing to such Employees;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(m)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any duties, taxes, interest and penalties levied by a Governmental
Authority relating to any importation or exportation of Purchased Assets that
occurred prior to the Effective Time;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(n)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

for goods and services provided to the Purchased Business prior to the Effective

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(o)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
product warranty, product liability and other claims and obligations
respecting products sold by the Vendor in connection with the Purchased Business
up to the Effective Time.</p>

</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">

acknowledges that the Purchaser is relying on such representations and
warranties in connection with its purchase of the Purchased Assets:</p>

organized and validly existing under the laws of the Province of Ontario, is in
good standing and has all necessary power and capacity to carry on the business
presently conducted by it, to own and dispose of the Purchased Assets, to
execute and deliver this Agreement and to carry out the terms and conditions of
this Agreement to the full extent.</font></p>

under the Transitional Services Agreement, together with the Purchased

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All of the Purchased Assets are in good condition and, if applicable, are

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
During the two years preceding the Execution Date, there has not been any
significant interruption of operations (being an interruption of more than one
day) of the Purchased Business due to inadequate maintenance of machinery or
equipment included in the Purchased Assets.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
With the exception of Inventory In-Transit, all the tangible assets of
the Purchased Business are situated at the National Logistics Services
warehouses, the Head Office and at the locations set out in Schedule 17.</p>

to Purchased Assets</a></b></u></p>

<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify">(</font></font><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

on the Financial Statements, other than assets acquired since the date of the

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

&quot;Leased<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">Stores&quot;</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">).</font></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></p>
  </font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All fixtures, improvements and appurtenances situated on the Leased
Stores are in good operating condition and in a state of good maintenance and
repair and are adequate and suitable for the purposes for which they are
currently being used.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
None of the Leased Stores fixtures or any equipment therein, nor the
operation or maintenance thereof, violates any provision of any Store Lease or
any provision of any Laws.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 6, the Vendor occupies, and has the
exclusive right to occupy and use, the Leased Stores.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Leased Stores, the current uses thereof and the conduct of the
Purchased Business comply with all Laws, including, without limitation, those
dealing with zoning, parking, access, loading facilities, landscaped areas,
building construction, fire and public health and safety and Environmental Laws;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
No alteration, repair, improvement or other work has been ordered,
directed or requested in writing to be done or performed to or in respect of the
Leased Stores or to any of the plumbing, heating, elevating, water, drainage or
electrical systems, fixtures or works by any Governmental Authority, which
alteration, repair, improvement or other work has not been completed, if it is a
responsibility of the Vendor Group under a Store Lease and to the Knowledge of
the Vendor, no written notification has been given to it of any such outstanding
work being ordered, directed or requested, other than those which have been
complied with;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All accounts for work and services performed and materials placed or
furnished upon or in respect of the Leased Stores at the request or on behalf of
the Vendor have been or will be fully paid and satisfied by the Vendor Group,
and no Person is entitled to claim a lien under the <i>Construction Lien Act</i>
(Ontario), as the same may be amended from time to time, any successor
legislation thereto or any analogous legislation in force in all other
jurisdictions of Canada in which the Vendor carries on business, against the
Leased Stores or any part thereof, other than current accounts in respect of
which the payment due date has not yet passed.&nbsp; Schedule 6 contains a list of
all amounts owed by the Vendor Group for work and services performed and
materials placed or furnished upon or in respect of the Leased Stores ;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
There is nothing owing in respect of the Leased Stores by the Vendor to
any municipal corporation or to any other corporation or commission owning or
operating a public utility for water, gas, electrical power or energy, steam or
hot water, or for the use thereof other than current accounts in respect of
which the payment due date has not yet passed;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Each of the Leased Stores is fit for its present use, and there are no
material or structural repairs or replacements which are necessary or advisable
and, without limiting the foregoing, there are no repairs to, or replacements of
the roof or the mechanical, electrical, heating, ventilating, air-conditioning,
plumbing or drainage equipment or systems which to the Knowledge of the Vendor
are necessary or advisable; and none of the Leased Stores is currently
undergoing any alteration or renovation nor is any such alteration or renovation
contemplated.</p>
</blockquote>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Ref87715102">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>5.10</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Store Leases</b></u></font></a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87966893">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor is not a party to any lease or agreement to lease in respect
of any real property, whether as lessor or lessee, other than the leases (the "</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">Store
Leases</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">")</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"> </font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">relating to the Leased Stores, as described in Schedule 6.&nbsp;
Schedule 6 sets out the parties to each of the Store Leases, any amendments
thereto, their respective dates of execution and expiry dates, any options to
renew, the locations of the leased lands and premises and the rent payable thereunder.</font></a><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></p>
  </font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Each of the Store Leases is in good standing and in full force and
effect, and neither the Vendor nor to the Knowledge of the Vendor, any other
party thereto is in breach of any covenants, conditions or obligations contained
therein.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as set out in Schedule 6, none of the Store Leases contain
provisions in the nature of the following:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
deeming a breach or default thereunder to be a default under one or more
other Store Leases;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
rights of termination in favour of a landlord in circumstances other than
upon a default by the tenant that has not been cured;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
obligation on the tenant to restore the condition of the premises to its
original state; or</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the relocation of the Leased Store.</p>
  </blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
A Store Lease Summary for each Store Lease has been prepared by the
Vendor and delivered to the Purchaser.&nbsp; Each Store Lease Summary provides an
accurate and complete summary of the matters set forth in respect of the
applicable Store Lease. </p>
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
With respect to the Store Leases:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
none of them have been altered or amended and has not been terminated or
surrendered and is unmodified;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
each of them fully discloses all aspects of the rights of the landlord
and tenant against each other and there are no collateral representations,
warranties or other obligations except as set out therein.</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Vendor has no claim for the repayment of any monies paid by it
pursuant to the Store Lease on account of minimum rent, additional rent or
otherwise. The Vendor has no claim, charge, lien, or right of set off for
damages or any other claim against the landlord with respect to the minimum
rent, additional rent or other amounts due or to become due under the Store
Lease, except in the ordinary course<b>;</b></p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
except as set forth in the Store Lease, the Vendor has not been afforded
any free rent, partial rent, rent rebates, rent abatements or rent concessions
of any kind (collectively, the "<b>Rent</b> <b>Concessions</b>") and all Rent
Concessions, if any, have been realized by the Vendor and full rent is now being
paid by the Vendor.</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(v)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any improvements, alterations, construction and build-outs required by
the terms of the Store Lease to be made by the landlord and the Vendor have been
made, and all tenant allowances, inducements and other payments, if any,
required to be paid to the Vendor by the landlord have been paid in full, except
as set forth in the Store Lease; </p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(vi)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
there is no litigation or governmental or municipal proceeding commenced,
or to the Knowledge of the Vendor pending or threatened against the Vendor with
respect to the Store Lease or the premises demised thereunder;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(vii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
none of them has been assigned nor has the whole or any part of the
Leased Store been sublet or licensed to another Person by the Vendor; and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(viii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
since taking possession of the Leased Store, the Vendor has not stored,
generated, manufactured, refined, treated, transported, disposed or in any way
used materials which are considered Hazardous Substances under applicable
Environmental Laws at the Leased Store, except for de minimus quantities
incidental to the cleaning or operation of Vendor's business.</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ix)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Vendor has not granted to the landlord a security interest in the
property of the Vendor used in connection with the business operated from the
Leased Store demised thereunder, which property constitutes Purchased Assets, as
security for the performance of the Vendor's obligations under the Store Lease
or otherwise, either under the Store Lease or by any separate agreement or
instrument;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(x)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
all leasing and other commissions or other payments required to be made
to leasing real estate agents or others on or before the Closing Date for
securing any Store Lease, excluding renewals thereof, have been or will be paid
in full and there exist no outstanding obligations of the Vendor with respect
thereto, which are or might be the responsibility or for the account of the
Purchaser; and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(xi)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Vendor has not received any notice that the landlord has assigned the
Store Lease or the rent payable thereunder to another Person.</p>
  </blockquote>
</blockquote>

<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">

</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The inventory levels of the Vendor have
been maintained at such amounts as are required for the operation of the
Purchased Business as previously conducted and as proposed to be conducted by
the Vendor, and such inventory levels are adequate therefor.</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p></font><a name="_Toc88578167">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>5.12</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">

</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight: normal">The Vendor does not carry on business,
and the Purchased Business is not operated, at any location other than as shown
in Schedule 17. </font> </p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>5.13</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"><u><b>Location of Purchased Inventory</b></u></font></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font></p>

Schedule
17.</p>
<p><a name="_Toc88578170">
<b>5.14</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Intellectual Property</b></u></a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Schedule 5 and Schedule 15 contain an accurate, complete and
comprehensive list of all Intellectual Property registered or applied for by the
Vendor Group in respect of the Purchased Business, setting out, in detail, the
relevant dates, reference numbers and jurisdictions of each, being acquired
hereunder.&nbsp; The Vendor Group has all necessary rights and is fully entitled to
grant, transfer, assign, sell and convey all rights in and to the Intellectual
Property as provided hereunder.&nbsp; The execution, delivery and performance of this
Agreement does not constitute nor will constitute a breach of any of the
Intellectual Property of the Vendor nor will result in a breach of, constitute a
default under, or requirement limitations of any contractual obligation of the
Vendor.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor Group is the beneficial owner of the Intellectual Property,
free and clear of all Encumbrances, other than Permitted Encumbrances, and,
other than shrink-wrap license agreements for "off-the-shelf" software, is not a
party to or bound by any Contract or any other obligation whatsoever that limits
or impairs its ability to sell, transfer, assign or convey, or that otherwise
affects, the Intellectual Property, subject to obtaining consents to transfer
under Contracts included in the Intellectual Property. No Person has been
granted any interest in or right to use all or any portion of the Intellectual
Property.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as set forth in Schedule 19, the conduct of the Purchased Business
does not infringe upon the intellectual property rights, domestic or foreign, of
any other Person and there are no claims against the Vendor asserting any
infringement or breach of any intellectual property rights of any other Person,
nor has the Vendor received any notice that the conduct of the Purchased
Business, including the use of the Intellectual Property, infringes upon or
breaches any intellectual property rights of any other Person, and to the
Knowledge of the Vendor, no Person has infringed or violated of any of its
rights in the Intellectual Property.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
To the Knowledge of the Vendor there is no state of facts which casts
doubt on the validity or enforceability of any of the Intellectual Property.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has provided to the Purchaser a true and complete copy of all
material written Contracts and amendments thereto which comprise or relate to
the Intellectual Property.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has used its reasonable efforts to take precautions and to
protect the proprietary Technical Information and other proprietary information
relating to the Purchased Business.&nbsp; The proprietary Technical Information has
not been disclosed to any other Person other than the Purchaser, its authorized
agents and Persons bound by an obligation of confidentiality.&nbsp; </p>
</blockquote>
</font>
<font style="font-weight: normal; ">
<p></font></font><a name="_Toc88578171">
<font style="font-weight: normal; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>5.15</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-weight: normal; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<u><b>Computer Programs</b></u></font></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none"></p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor takes commercially reasonable precautions to protect the
integrity of the Computer Programs used in the Purchased Business. </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The documentation provided by the Vendor in respect of the Computer
Programs is sufficient to allow the Purchaser, with the assistance of skilled
software professionals possessing experience in this industry and sufficient
knowledge of the Computer Programs, to operate the Purchased Business.</p>
</blockquote>
<p><a name="_Toc88578172">
<b>5.16</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Insurance</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has the Purchased Assets insured against loss or damage by all
insurable hazards or risks on a replacement cost basis and such insurance
coverage will be continued in full force and effect to and including the Time of
Closing.</p>
<p class="Article1L3">(b)<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Schedule 18 sets out a summary of all insurance policies (specifying the
insurer, deductibles, the amount of the coverage, termination/renewal dates, the
type of insurance, the policy number and any pending claims thereunder)
maintained by the Vendor on the Purchased Assets or personnel and true and
complete copies of the most recent inspection reports, if any, received from
insurance underwriters or others as to the condition of the Purchased Assets.</p>
<p class="Article1L3">(c)<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor is not in default with respect to any of the provisions
contained in any such insurance policy and has not failed to give any notice or
present any claim under any such insurance policy in a due and timely fashion.</p>
<p class="Article1L3">(d)<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor will provide a true copy of each insurance policy referred to
in Schedule 18 to the Purchaser prior to the Closing Date.</p>
</blockquote>
<p><a name="_Toc88578173">
<b>5.17</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>No Expropriation</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">No part of the Purchased Assets has been
taken or expropriated by any Governmental Authority, nor has any notice or
proceeding in respect thereof been given or commenced, nor to the Knowledge of
the Vendor is there any intent or proposal to give any such notice or commence
any such proceedings.</p>
</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; ">

<font style="font-weight: normal; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>5.18</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="text-decoration: underline; font-weight:normal; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><u><b>Agreements and Commitments</b></u></font></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font></p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="text-decoration: none">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font></font><font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Other than the Assumed Contracts and as set forth in Schedule 8, the
Vendor is not a party to or bound by any Contract of the Purchased Business or
the Purchased Assets, including without limitation:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any distributor, sales, advertising, agency or manufacturer's
representative Contract;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any collective bargaining agreement, voluntary recognition agreement,
statutory duty to collective bargain towards a collective agreement or other
Contract with any labour union;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any written employment or consulting Contract or any other written
Contract with any officer, employee or consultant;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any profit sharing, bonus, stock option, pension, retirement, disability,
stock purchase, medical, dental, hospitalization, insurance or similar plan or
agreement providing benefits to any current or former director, officer,
employee or consultant;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(v)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any trust indenture, mortgage, promissory note, loan agreement, guarantee
or other Contract for the borrowing of money or a leasing transaction of the
type required to be capitalized in accordance with generally accepted accounting
principles;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(vi)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any commitment for charitable contributions other than gift boxes for The
Kids Help Phone;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(vii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any Contract for the sale of any assets, other than sales of inventory to
customers in the ordinary course of the Purchased Business;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(viii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any confidentiality, secrecy or nondisclosure Contract (whether the
Vendor is a beneficiary or obligor thereunder) relating to any proprietary or
confidential information or any non-competition or similar Contract;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ix)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any licence, franchise or other agreement which relates in whole or in
part to any Intellectual Property or to the Purchased Business.</p>
  </blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Assumed Contracts are used to operate the Purchased Business.
</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has performed all of the obligations required to be performed
by it and is entitled to all benefits under, and is not in default or alleged to
be in default in respect of, any Assumed Contract.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All of the Assumed Contracts are in good standing and in full force and
effect, and subject to obtaining required consents, no event, condition or
occurrence exists which, after notice or lapse of time or both, would constitute
a default under any of the foregoing.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 10, none of the Material Contracts
contain provisions providing for the automatic renewal of the Contract or
permitting changes to the terms thereof as a result of an assignment of the
Contract.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Schedule 10 provides an accurate summary of the Material Contracts.&nbsp;
</p>
</blockquote>

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

respects with all Laws applicable to the Purchased Business and the Purchased

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Financial Statements have been prepared in accordance with generally

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<b>5.24</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
