</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72">Since the date of Financial Statements
and except as disclosed in Schedule 12, the Purchased Business has been carried
on only in the ordinary and normal course consistent with past practice and
there has not been:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any Material Adverse Change;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
other than damaged inventory (which is excluded from the "<b>Purchased
Assets</b>") any damage, destruction or loss (whether or not covered by
insurance) affecting the Purchased Business and/or the Purchased Assets,
reasonable wear and tear accepted.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any obligation or liability (whether absolute, accrued, contingent or
otherwise, and whether due or to become due) incurred by the Vendor in
connection with the Purchased Business, other than those incurred in the
ordinary and normal course of the Purchased Business and consistent with past
practice;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any payment, discharge or satisfaction of any Encumbrance, liability or
obligation of the Vendor in relation to the Purchased Business or the Purchased
Assets (whether absolute, accrued, contingent or otherwise, and whether due or
to become due) other than payment of accounts payable and tax liabilities
incurred in the ordinary and normal course of business consistent with past
practice;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

Business or the Purchased Assets, including without limitation, any complaint,
investigation or charge under applicable Employment Legislation;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

on or over any Purchased Assets, other than sales of inventory to customers in
the ordinary and normal course of the Purchased Business;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

(including, without limitation, any increase pursuant to any Employee Plan or
commitment), or any increase in any such compensation or bonus payable to any
officer, Employee, consultant or agent thereof (having an annual salary or
remuneration in excess of $30,000) or the execution of any employment contract
with any officer or employee (having an annual salary or remuneration in excess
of $30,000), or the making of any loan to, or engagement in any transaction
with, any employee, officer or director of the Vendor in relation to the
Purchased Business;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

Business or Purchased Assets in excess of $10,000 in the aggregate;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(i)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(j)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(k)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(l)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(m)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><a name="_Toc88578181">
<b>5.25</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Non-Arm's Length Transactions</b></u></font></a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" style="page-break-after: avoid; text-indent:72">With
respect to the Purchased Business, except as set out in Schedule 14:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Vendor has not since the date of the Financial Statements made any payment
or loan to, or borrowed any moneys from or is otherwise indebted to, any
officer, director, employee, shareholder or any other Person not dealing at
arm's length with the Vendor (within the meaning of the <i>Tax Act</i>) or any
Affiliate or Associate of any of the foregoing, except as disclosed on the
Financial Statements and except for usual employee reimbursements and
compensation paid in the ordinary course of the Purchased Business;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Vendor has not received and does not receive or use any ongoing services,
rights or goods from any non arm's length Person, except management services,
warehousing and logistics services, information technology services, importation
services, legal services, lease administration services and gift card services; </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
except for Contracts of employment, the Vendor is not a party to any Contract
with any officer, director, Employee, shareholder or any other Person not
dealing at arm's length with the Vendor (within the meaning of the <i>Tax Act</i>)
or any Affiliate or Associate of any of the foregoing;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
No officer, director or shareholder of the Vendor and no entity which is an
Affiliate or Associate of one or more of such individuals:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
owns, directly or indirectly, any interest in (except for shares representing
less than one per cent of the outstanding shares of any class or series of any
publicly traded company), or is an officer, director, employee or consultant of,
any Person which is, or is engaged in business as, a competitor of the Purchased
Business or a lessor, lessee, supplier, distributor, sales agent or customer of
the Purchased Business;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
owns, directly or indirectly, in whole or in part, any property that the Vendor
uses in the operations of the Purchased Business, except to the extent that the
benefit of which will be provided to the Purchaser pursuant to the Transitional
Services Agreement; or</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
has any cause of action or other claim whatsoever against, or owes any amount
to, any member of the Vendor Group in connection with the Purchased Business,
except for any liabilities reflected in the Financial Statements and claims in
the ordinary course of business such as for accrued vacation pay and accrued
benefits under Employee Plans.</p>
  </blockquote>
</blockquote>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<p></font><a name="_Ref87715426">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>5.26</b></font></a></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font><a name="_Ref87715426"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Taxes</b></u></font></font></a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Each member of the Vendor Group has duly filed on a timely basis all Tax
Returns required to be filed by them and has paid all Taxes which are due and
payable, and all assessments, reassessments, governmental charges, penalties,
interest and fines due and payable by it.</p>
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has made adequate provision for Taxes payable in respect of
the Purchased Business for the current period and any previous period for which
Tax Returns are not yet required to be filed.</p>
  </font>
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
There are no actions, suits, proceedings, investigations or claims
pending or, to the Knowledge of the Vendor, threatened against the Vendor in
respect of Taxes, governmental charges or assessments, nor are any material
matters under discussion with any Governmental Authority relating to Taxes,
governmental charges or assessments asserted by any such authority.</p>
  </font>
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has withheld from each payment made to any of its past or
present employees, officers or directors, and to any non-resident of Canada, the
amount of all Taxes and other deductions required to be withheld therefrom, and
has paid the same to the proper tax or other receiving officers within the time
required under any applicable legislation.</p>
  </font>
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
  <font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has remitted to the appropriate tax authority, when required
by law to do so, all amounts collected by it on account of Taxes, including
without limitation, provincial sales taxes, harmonized taxes and GST.</p>
</blockquote>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">

</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Litigation</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87715345">
(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 19, there are no:</a></p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
actions, suits or proceedings, at law or in equity, by any Person,</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
arbitration or alternative dispute resolution process, or</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
administrative or other proceeding or, to the Knowledge of the Vendor,
threatened against or affecting the Vendor at law or in equity or before or by
any Governmental Authority,</p>
  </blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; in respect of or affecting the Purchased
Business and/or the Purchased Assets.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
To the Knowledge of the Vendor there is no ground on which any action
referred to in subsection 5.27(a)<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003300340035000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->, or a suit or proceeding might be commenced with any
reasonable likelihood of success.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor is not subject to any judgment, order or decree entered in any
lawsuit or proceeding nor has the Vendor settled any claim prior to being
prosecuted in respect of it.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as disclosed in Schedule 19, the Vendor is not the plaintiff or
complainant in any act, suit or proceeding arising out of or affecting the
Purchased Business;</p>
</blockquote>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">

the purposes of the Tax Act.</p>

</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font>

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">The Vendor is a registrant for purposes
of the ETA whose registration number is 865278907RT0001;</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight:normal"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
<b>5.30</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Environmental</b></u></font></font></a></p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"></font></font></font></font></font>
</font></font><a name="_Ref87714809">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
(a)</font>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 22, the Vendor, in respect of the
Purchased Business and the Purchased Assets, has been and is in compliance with
all Laws, directives and decisions rendered by any ministry, department or
administrative or regulatory agency ("</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">Environmental Laws</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">") relating to
the protection of the environment, occupational health and safety or the
manufacture, processing, distribution, use, treatment, storage, disposal,
discharge, transport or handling of any pollutants, contaminants, chemicals or
industrial toxic or hazardous wastes or substances ("</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">Hazardous Substances</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">");</font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; "></p>
  </font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<a name="_Ref87714823">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
(b)</font>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has obtained all licences, permits, approvals, consents,
certificates, registrations and other authorizations under Environmental Laws
(the "<b>Environmental Permits</b>") required for the operation of the Purchased
Business. Each Environmental Permit is valid, subsisting and in good standing,
and the Vendor is not in default or breach of any Environmental Permit and no
proceeding is pending or threatened to revoke or limit any Environmental Permit;</a></p>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor, in connection with the Purchased Business, has not used or
permitted to be used, except in compliance with all Environmental Laws, any of
its property (including the Leased Stores);</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
To the Knowledge of the Vendor, no Leased Store is or ever has been
insulated with urea formaldehyde insulation, nor do such buildings or structures
contain any aluminium wiring or friable asbestos or any other substance
containing asbestos;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has never received any notice of, or been prosecuted for an
offence alleging, non-compliance with any Environmental Laws, nor has the Vendor
settled any allegation of non-compliance short of prosecution. There are no
orders or directions relating to environmental matters requiring any work,
repairs, construction or capital expenditures to be made with respect to the
Purchased Business or the Purchased Assets, nor has the Vendor received notice
of any of the same;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as disclosed in Schedule 22, to the Knowledge of the Vendor, there
are no pending or proposed changes to Environmental Laws which would render
illegal or restrict the manufacture or sale of any product manufactured or sold
or any service provided by the Vendor in connection with the Purchased Business;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has not caused or permitted the release, in any manner
whatsoever, of any Hazardous Substance on or from any of its properties or
assets (including the Leased Stores) utilized in the Purchased Business, or any
such release on or from a facility which it previously owned or leased, or any
such release on or from a facility owned or operated by third parties but with
respect to which the Vendor in connection with the Purchased Business is or may
reasonably be alleged to have liability. All Hazardous Substances and all other
wastes and other materials and substances used in whole or in part by the Vendor
in connection with the Purchased Business or resulting from the Purchased
Business have been disposed of, treated and stored in compliance with all
Environmental Laws. Schedule 22 identifies all of the locations where Hazardous
Substances used in whole or in part by the Vendor in connection with the
Purchased Business have been or are being stored or disposed of;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor has not received any notice that it is potentially responsible
for a federal, provincial, municipal or local clean-up site or corrective action
under any Environmental Laws in connection with the Purchased Business. The
Vendor, in connection with the Purchased Business, has not received any request
for information in connection with any federal, provincial, municipal or local
inquiries as to disposal sites; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
To the Knowledge of the Vendor, there are no environmental audits,
evaluations, assessments, studies or tests relating to the Purchased Business or
Purchased Assets.</p>
</blockquote>

</font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font>
</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<b>5.32</b></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Employee Plans</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87956672">(</a></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; "><a name="_Ref87956672">a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Schedule 13 identifies each retirement, pension, bonus, stock purchase,
profit sharing, stock option, deferred compensation, severance or termination
pay, insurance, medical, hospital, dental, vision care, drug, sick leave,
disability, salary continuation, legal benefits, unemployment benefits,
vacation, incentive or other compensation plan or arrangement or other employee
benefit which is maintained, or otherwise contributed to or required to be
contributed to, by the Vendor relating to the Purchased Business or the
Purchased Assets for the benefit of Employees or former employees of the Vendor
(the "<b>Employee Plans</b>")</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87949649">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
A true and complete copy of each Employee Plan has been furnished to the
Purchaser.</a> </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Each Employee Plan has been maintained in compliance with its terms and
with the requirements prescribed by any Laws that are applicable to such
Employee Plan.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 13:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
all contributions to, and payments from, each Employee Plan which may
have been required to be made in accordance with the terms of any such Employee
Plan, or with the recommendation of the actuary for such Employee Plan, and,
where applicable, the Laws of the jurisdictions which govern such Employee Plan,
have been made in a timely manner;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
all material reports, returns and similar documents (including
applications for approval of contributions) with respect to any Employee Plan
required to be filed with any Governmental Authority or distributed to any
Employee Plan participant have been duly filed in a timely manner or
distributed;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
there are no pending investigations by any Governmental Authority
involving or relating to any Employee Plan, no threatened or pending claims
(except for claims for benefits payable in the normal operation of the Employee
Plans), suits or proceedings against any Employee Plan or asserting any rights
or claims to benefits under any Employee Plan which could give rise to a
liability nor, to the Knowledge of the Vendor, are there any facts that could
give rise to any liability in the event of such investigation, claim, suit or
proceeding;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
no notice has been received by the Vendor of any complaints or other
proceedings of any kind involving the Vendor or, to the Knowledge of the Vendor,
any of the Employees before any Governmental Authority, pension board or
committee relating to any Employee Plan or to the Purchased Business or the
Purchased Assets; and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(v)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
if applicable, the assets of each Employee Plan are at least equal to the
liabilities of such Employee Plan based on the actuarial assumptions utilized in
the most recent valuation performed by the actuary for such Employee Plan, and
neither the Purchaser nor any of its Associates or Affiliates will incur any
liability with respect to any Employee Plan as a result of the transactions
contemplated by this Agreement.</p>
  </blockquote>
</blockquote>

</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u>Employees</u></font></font></a></b></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87956706">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Schedule 13 contains a complete and accurate list of the names of all
Head Office Employees presently employed by the Vendor.&nbsp; Within three Business
Days following the Execution Date, the Vendor shall provide to the Purchaser a
list of the names of all individuals who are full-time, part-time or casual
employees or individuals engaged on contract to provide employment services or
sales or other agents or representatives of the Vendor employed or engaged in
the Purchased Business (the "<b>Employees</b>") (other than the Excluded
Employees) specifying the length of hire, title or classification and rate of
salary or hourly pay and commission or bonus entitlements (if any) for each such
Employee.</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87956269">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor shall also provide to the Purchaser, Within three Business
Days following the Execution Date, a list of all Employees who are presently not
at work, including without limitation, those on lay-off as well as those in
receipt of benefits under the Workplace Safety Act, long-term disability,
statutorily authorized leave (collectively, the "<b>Absent Employees</b>") as
well as the reason for their absence, the last day worked and the expected date
of return to work.</a> </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 13, there are no complaints, claims or
charges outstanding, or to the Knowledge of the Vendor, anticipated, nor are
there any orders, decisions, directions or convictions currently registered or
outstanding by any tribunal or agency against or in respect of the Vendor under
or in respect of any Employment Legislation.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
There are no appeals pending before the WSIB or the Workplace Safety and
Insurance Tribunal involving the Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All levies, assessments and penalties made against the Vendor pursuant to
the Workplace Safety Act have been paid by the Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
There has been no change in the rating assessment applicable to the
Vendor or the Purchased Business under such legislation during the past five
years, except as described in Schedule 13;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
to the Knowledge of the Vendor, no investigation or audit is currently
being performed by the WSIB or any other Governmental Authority; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
all payments required to be made in trust to the Director of Employment
Standards in respect of termination and/or severance pay under the Employment
Legislation in respect of the Employees have been made.</p>
</blockquote>

<a name="_Toc88578193">Article 6<br>

TO THE TRADEMARK VENDOR</a></p>

<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">

and severally represents and warrants to the Purchaser as follows and
acknowledge that the Purchaser is relying on such representations and warranties
in connection with its purchase of the Purchased Trademarks:</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight:normal; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

</font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration: none">The Trademark Vendor is incorporated and
validly subsisting under the laws of the State of Nevada, is in good standing
and has all necessary corporate power and capacity to carry on the business
presently conducted by it, to own and dispose of the Purchased Trademarks, to
execute and deliver this Agreement and to carry out the terms and conditions of
this Agreement to the full extent.</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight:normal">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

and delivered by the Trademark Vendor and is a legal, valid and binding
obligation of the Trademark Vendor, enforceable against it by the Purchaser in

insolvency and other laws affecting the rights of creditors generally and except

<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578198">
<b>6.5</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>No Violation</b></u></a></p>
</font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration: none">The execution and delivery of this
Agreement by the Trademark Vendor and the consummation of the transactions
herein provided for will not result in:</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the breach or violation of any of the provisions to or constitute a
default under, or conflict with or cause the acceleration of any obligation of
the Trademark Vendor under:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any Contract to which the Trademark Vendor is a party or by which it is
or its properties are bound;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any provision of the constating documents or by-laws or resolutions of
the board of directors (or any committee thereof) or shareholders of the
Trademark Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any judgment, decree, order or award of any court, Governmental Authority
or arbitrator having jurisdiction over the Trademark Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any licence, permit, approval, consent or authorization held by the
Trademark Vendor; or</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(v)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any Laws;</p>
  </blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the creation or imposition of any Encumbrance on any of the Purchased
Trademarks.</p>
</blockquote>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87715448">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>6.6</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"><u><b>Title to Purchased Trademarks</b></u></font></font></a></p>
</font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">The Principal Trademarks, including all
goodwill associated therewith, are legally and beneficially owned by the
Trademark Vendor with good and marketable title thereto, free and clear of all
Encumbrances, and, to the Knowledge of the Trademark Vendor, the other Purchased
Trademarks, whether unregistered, pending or registered, including all goodwill
associated therewith, are legally and beneficially owned by the Trademark Vendor
with good and marketable title thereto, free and clear of all Encumbrances.</font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<b>6.7</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <font style="text-decoration: underline">

<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">The use of the Principal Trademarks does
not infringe upon or breach any intellectual property rights of any Person, and
to the Knowledge of the Trademark Vendor, no Person has infringed or violated
any of its rights in the Principal Trademarks.</font></font></p>

<blockquote>

(</a></font></font><a name="_Ref87715365"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Except as described in Schedule 19, there are no:</font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"></p>

<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

or by any Governmental Authority,</p>
  </blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; in respect of or affecting the Trademark

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

action referred to in subsection 6.11(a)<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>

</xml><![endif]-->, or suit or proceeding might be commenced with any reasonable
likelihood of success.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

entered in any lawsuit or proceeding nor has the Vendor settled any claim prior

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

severally represent and warrant to the Purchaser as follows and acknowledge that
the Purchaser is relying on such representations and warranties in connection
with its purchase of the Purchased Assets and the Purchased Trademarks:</font></p>

</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; American Eagle Canada</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">.
American Eagle Canada is incorporated and validly subsisting under the laws of
the Province of Nova Scotia, is in good standing and has all necessary corporate
power and capacity to carry on the business presently conducted by it, to own
and dispose of its assets, to execute and deliver this Agreement and to carry
out the terms and conditions of this Agreement to the full extent.</p>
  </font>

<p class="Article1L1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">
<a name="_Toc88578224">Article 10<br>
COVENANTS</a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87715530">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>10.1</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Access to Purchased Business</b></u></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor and the Trademark Vendor shall forthwith make available to the
Purchaser and its authorized representatives and, if requested by the Purchaser,
provide a copy to the Purchaser of all title documents, Contracts, financial
statements, policies, plans, reports, licences, orders, permits, books of
account, accounting records and all other documents, information and data
relating to the Purchased Business, the Purchased Assets and the Purchased
Trademarks.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At the request of the Purchaser, the Vendor shall afford the Purchaser
and its authorized representatives every reasonable opportunity to have free and
unrestricted access to the Purchased Assets and all other property and assets
utilized in the Purchased Business.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At the request of the Purchaser, the Vendor and the Trademark Vendor
shall execute such consents, authorizations and directions as may be necessary
to permit any inspection of the Purchased Business, any of the Purchased Assets
or the Purchased Trademarks to enable the Purchaser or its authorized
representatives to obtain full access to all files and records relating to any
of the Purchased Assets and the Purchased Trademarks maintained by any
Governmental Authority.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
At the Purchaser's request, the Vendor and the Trademark Vendor shall
co-operate with the Purchaser in arranging any such meetings as the Purchaser
should reasonably request with:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Employees;</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
customers, suppliers, distributors or others who have or have had a
business relationship with the Vendor in respect of the Purchased Business; and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the auditors, solicitors or any other persons engaged or previously
engaged to provide services to the Vendor or the Trademark Vendor who have
knowledge of matters relating to the Purchased Business, Purchased Assets or the
Purchased Trademarks. In particular, without limitation, the Vendor shall permit
the Purchaser's representatives or consultants to conduct all such testing and
inspection in respect of environmental matters at such locations of the
Purchased Business as the Purchaser may determine, in its sole discretion, as
may be required to satisfy the Purchaser in respect of such matters, provided
that the Purchaser shall cause no damage to any location of the Purchased
Business, and the Vendor shall conduct, in co-operation with the representatives
or consultants of the Purchaser, such physical review of the Purchased Assets as
is necessary so as to enable the confirmation of the values carried on the
balance sheets of the Vendor in respect of such assets, to the reasonable
satisfaction of the Purchaser.</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The exercise of any rights of inspection by or on behalf of the Purchaser
under this section 10.1<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003500330030000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> shall not mitigate or otherwise affect any of the
representations and warranties of the other Parties to this Agreement hereunder
which shall continue in full force and effect as provided in section 9.1<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003500350035000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->.</p>
  </blockquote>
</blockquote>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578226">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>10.2</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Return of Computer Hardware and Computer
Programs</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="justify">
<a name="_Toc88578227">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; At the request of the Purchaser, the Computer Programs
owned by the Vendor located in Warrendale, PA, will be returned to the Head
Office at the Vendor's expense.&nbsp; </font> </a></p>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578228">
<b>10.3</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Transitional Services</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" style="text-indent: 72" align="justify">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration: none">On the Closing Date, in conjunction with
the consummation of the transactions contemplated in this Agreement, the Vendor
and the Purchaser shall enter into a transitional services agreement, on terms
satisfactory to the Purchaser and the Vendor (the "Transitional
Services Agreement"), for the purpose of achieving the segregation of the
American Eagle operations from the operations of the Purchased Business, the
relocation of the operations of the Purchased Business to the Head Office and
the operation of the Purchased Business on and following the Closing Date,
including without limitation, the transition of operating systems, performance
of payroll processing services, lease administration and information technology
services and the operation and sale of inventory at the Excluded Leased Store,
such agreement to be for such period of time as the Purchaser shall require.&nbsp;
</font></font>
</p>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font></font><a name="_Toc88578229">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>10.4</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Consent to Assign Store Leases</b></u></a></p>
</font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">The Purchaser shall use commercially
reasonable efforts, without an obligation to incur any financial costs, to
obtain, at or prior to the Time of Closing,
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
landlord consents to the assignment of the Store Leases described in
Schedule 21 by the Vendor to the Purchaser on
terms and conditions acceptable to the Purchaser, in its sole discretion. </font>
</font>
</p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"> <font style="color: black">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font></font><a name="_Ref87966965">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>10.5</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<u><b>Xerox Lease</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">On the Closing Date, in conjunction with
the consummation of the transactions contemplated in this Agreement, the Vendor
and the Purchaser shall enter into a sublease of the Xerox Lease (the "Xerox
Sublease"), or terms and conditions satisfactory to the Vendor and the
Purchaser, pursuant to which the Purchaser will obtain the benefits of the
Vendor under the Xerox Lease for a period of at least nine months, terminable at
the option of the Purchaser following such nine month period upon thirty days
notice to the Vendor.&nbsp; Upon the expiry of the Xerox Sublease, the Purchaser
shall have no further obligations to the Vendor in respect of the Xerox
Lease.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font></font> </p>
<font style="color: black">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font></font><a name="_Toc88578231">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>10.6</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Release under Store Leases</b></u></a></p>
</font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">The Purchaser shall use commercially
reasonable efforts to obtain, within fourteen days following the Execution Date,
the release of the Vendor and its Affiliates from all obligations arising after
the Effective Time under those Store Leases representing at least 80% of the
Leased Stores in number, volume of sales and rent obligations.&nbsp; In the event the
Vendor is released from Store Leases for 80% of the Leased Stores in number,
volume of sales and rent obligations, the Vendor shall be solely responsible for
all of its expenses and consultants' fees incurred in connection with obtaining
the releases and the consents to the assignment of the Store Leases referred to
in Schedule 21, otherwise the Vendor and the Purchaser shall each be responsible
to pay one half of such expenses and fees of the Vendor. </font></font> </p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"> <font style="color: black">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font></font><a name="_Ref88462151">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>10.7</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<u><b>Robson Street Store</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"></font></font>
<a name="_Ref88462152">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Parties acknowledge and agree that the Vendor will continue to
operate the Excluded Leased Store as a Bluenotes/Thriftys store following the
Closing Date until January 3, 2005 (the "</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">Interim Period").</font></font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;
</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor shall operate the Leased Store and conduct the business
therein in a manner generally consistent with the operations of the Purchaser
having regard to the Purchaser's pricing, promotion and sales practices but
taking into account the need to liquidate the inventory at the store before the
end of the Interim Period. </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Transitional Services Agreement will contain the terms of a license,
on a non-exclusive, royalty free basis, for the Vendor to use the "Bluenotes"
and "Thriftys" trademarks in connection with the operations at the Excluded
Leased Store during the Interim Period. </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor shall pay to the Purchaser, upon the expiry of the Interim
Period, an amount equal to the 25% of the Net Sale Proceeds of all inventory of
the Vendor Group sold at the Excluded Leased Store during the Interim Period.
</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Upon the expiry of the Interim Period, the Vendor shall sell, and the
Purchaser shall acquire, the remaining inventory located at the Excluded Leased
Store at a price equal to $1.55 per unit of inventory.&nbsp; The Purchaser shall
remove, at its cost, the acquired inventory from the Leased Stores upon the
expiry of the Interim Period.&nbsp; </p>
</blockquote>
</font></font>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578233">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>10.8</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><u><b>Inventory
Count</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<p align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<a name="_Toc88578234">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
On the close of business on the date immediately preceding the
Closing Date, the Vendor, or its agent, shall conduct a physical audit of the
Inventory On Hand and shall deliver to the Purchaser a statement summarizing the
actual Inventory On Hand in a format mutually agreed to with the Purchaser.&nbsp; The
Vendor shall consult with the Purchaser and collectively determine the manner in
which the inventory count will be performed.&nbsp; The costs incurred in connection
with the inventory audit shall be split equally between the Vendor and
Purchaser.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font> </a></p>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578235">
<b>10.9</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Payment of Purchased Inventory</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font>
</font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">The Vendor shall pay all amounts owing
to all suppliers or other third parties, when due, in connection with its
purchase of the Purchased Inventory.</font></font></font></font></font></p>
<font style="color: black">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578236">
<b>10.10</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Inventory On Order</b></u></a></p>
</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">The Purchaser shall cause to be issued
to the Vendor from its banker or other financial services institution a stand-by
letter of credit to reimburse the Vendor for its payment obligations to
suppliers of Inventory On Order. &nbsp;The stand-by letter of credit issued on behalf
of the Purchaser shall be of an amount equal to the aggregate amount of the
Vendor's outstanding letters of credit.&nbsp; In addition, to the extent that prior
to the Closing Date a supplier has drawn on any letter of credit issued by the
Vendor with respect to Inventory On Order, the Purchaser shall reimburse the
Vendor after Closing for such amount forthwith on notice from the Vendor of
same.&nbsp; </font></font></font></font> </p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"> <font style="color: black">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font></font><a name="_Ref88436622">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>10.11</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font>
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<u><b>Sales of Inventory</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The Purchaser covenants and agrees that
during the eight week period following the Closing Date:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
subject to this section 10.11<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380038003400330036003600320032000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->, it shall price and sell the Purchased Inventory in
accordance with the WAR Report;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
it will not discount the sale price of the Purchased Inventory otherwise
than in accordance with the WAR Report without the consent of the Vendor; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
it will not sell any inventory at the Leased Stores other than the
Purchased Inventory and the Inventory On Order.</p>
</blockquote>

On Order following Closing until such inventory is delivered to the Purchaser.&nbsp;

deliver to the Purchaser a complete and accurate list of all Permits held by or

<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
