<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578245">
<b>10.17</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Conduct of Purchased Business Prior to Closing</b></u></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">Without in any way limiting any other
obligations of the Vendor hereunder, during the period from the Execution Date
to the Time of Closing, except with the Purchaser's prior written consent:</font></font></font></font></font></font></p>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<font style="text-decoration: underline"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></font>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"> <font style="color: black">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font></font></font></font></font><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Conduct Business in the Ordinary Course.
The Vendor shall conduct the Purchased Business, and the Trademark Vendor shall
maintain the Purchased Trademarks, only in the ordinary and normal course
consistent with past practice and the Vendor and the Trademark Vendor shall not,
without the prior written consent of the Purchaser, enter into any transaction
or refrain from doing any action which, if effected before the Execution Date,
would constitute a breach of any representation, warranty, covenant or other
obligation of the Vendor or the Trademark Vendor contained herein, and the
Vendor shall not enter into any material supply arrangements relating to the
Purchased Business or make any material decisions or enter into any material
contracts with respect to the Purchased Business without the consent of the
Purchaser;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(</font></font></font></font><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">b)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font> </font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Continue Insurance.
The Vendor shall continue to maintain in full force and effect all policies of
insurance or renewals thereof now in effect, shall take out, at the expense of
the Purchaser, such additional insurance as may be reasonably requested by the
Purchaser and shall give all notices and present all claims under all policies
of insurance in a due and timely fashion;</p>
</font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; ">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Regulatory Consents</font></font><font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></font><font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">.
The Vendor, the Trademark Vendor and the Purchaser shall use their best efforts
to obtain, at or prior to the Time of Closing, from all appropriate Governmental
Authorities, the licences, permits, consents, approvals, certificates,
registrations and authorizations described in Schedule 20;</p>
</font></font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; ">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Contractual Consents</font></font><font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">.
The Vendor and the Purchaser shall use their best efforts to give or obtain, at
or prior to the Time of Closing, the notices, consents and approvals described
in Schedule 21 other than the necessary consents to the assignment of the Store
Leases;</p>
</font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font></font></font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Preserve Goodwill</font><font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">.
The Vendor and the Trademark Vendor shall each preserve intact the Purchased
Business, including the Purchased Assets and the Purchased Trademarks and to
carry on the Purchased Business as currently conducted, and they shall each
promote and preserve for the Purchaser the goodwill of suppliers, customers and
others having business relations with them;</p>
</font></font>
</font></font>
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">Continued Employment Terms</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">.&nbsp;
The Vendor shall continue to maintain its present practices with respect to the
present terms and conditions pertaining to each Employee. </p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Discharge Liabilities.
Except as otherwise required herein, the Vendor shall pay and discharge the
liabilities of the Vendor relating to the Purchased Business in the ordinary
course in accordance and consistent with the previous practice of the Vendor,
except those contested in good faith by the Vendor;</p>
</font></font>
</font></font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Inventory Orders</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">.
The Vendor shall not place any orders for inventory of the Purchased Business
without the prior approval of the Purchaser; </p>
</font>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Taxes.</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp; The
Vendor Group shall pay, when due, all Taxes which are due and payable;</p>
</font>
</font></font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(j)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Corporate Action</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">.
Each member of the Vendor Group shall use its best efforts to take or cause to
be taken all necessary corporate action, steps and proceedings to approve or
authorize validly and effectively the transfer of the Purchased Assets and the
Purchased Trademarks to the Purchaser and the execution and delivery of this
Agreement and the other agreements and documents contemplated hereby and to
cause all necessary meetings of directors and shareholders of the Vendor Group
to be held for such purpose; and</p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(k)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Best Efforts. The
Vendor and the Purchaser shall use their best efforts to satisfy the conditions
contained in Article 11<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>

</xml><![endif]-->.</p>
</blockquote>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"><b>10.23</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<u><b>Employees</b></u></p>
</font>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref88047892">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Prior to and effective on the Closing Date, the Purchaser shall offer
employment in writing to all of the Employees other than the Excluded Employees,
and the Purchaser shall offer employment to the Absent Employees effective on
the date of their return to work, on terms and conditions of employment,
including but not limited to, salaries, wages, incentive compensation and
benefits, which are substantially similar in the aggregate to the existing terms
and conditions of employment of the Employees immediately prior to the Closing
Date. Any Employee who accepts the Purchaser's offer of employment shall become
an employee of the Purchaser (the "</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">Transferred Employees</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">").</font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; ">&nbsp;
The service of the Transferred Employees as recognized by the Vendor shall be
recognized by the Purchaser for all purposes.&nbsp; The offer of employment to the
Head Office Employees who are governed by existing written employment agreements
with the Vendor shall contain a term that the Employee and the Purchaser will
continue to be bound by the termination/severance terms contained in the
Employee's existing employment agreement with the Vendor.&nbsp; The Head Office
Employees must execute the offer of employment letter prior to the Closing Date,
accepting the terms of the offer.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All costs, expenses and liabilities relating to the employment of those
Employees who do not accept the Purchaser's offer of employment and the
termination thereof, including without limitation, wages, severance pay, accrued
vacation pay, employee benefits, Taxes and all other amounts owing to such
Employees shall be paid and satisfied by the Vendor.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88040474">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser may terminate the employment of up to forty-six Head Office
Employees (the "<b>Terminated Employees</b>"), at any time following the Closing
Date but prior to </a>April 2<b>, </b>2005.&nbsp; The
Vendor shall be afforded an opportunity to transition Terminated Employees to
the Vendor's business prior to the termination of their employment.&nbsp; The Vendor
shall be responsible to pay all costs, expenses and liabilities (statutory or at
common law), including without limitation, termination pay and severance pay
relating to the termination of the employment of the Terminated Employees,
unless such costs, expenses or liabilities result from any act made by the
Purchaser in bad faith or in violation of any laws.&nbsp; The Purchaser shall prepare
the letter of termination for the Terminated Employees, subject to the prior
approval of the Vendor, and the Vendor shall, at its sole expense, be solely
responsible for negotiating the settlement of, or defending, any claims with
respect to termination pay and/or severance pay related to the Terminated
Employees.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88481752">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
All costs, expenses and liabilities relating to the employment of the
Transferred Employees including without limitation, wages, accrued vacation pay,
employee benefits, Taxes and all other amounts owing to the Transferred
Employees or otherwise accruing during or attributable to the period preceding
the Effective Time, shall be paid and satisfied by the Vendor on or prior to the
Closing Date or as part of the payroll next following such date.</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor shall indemnify and hold harmless the Purchaser from and
against all Losses suffered or incurred by the Purchaser as a result of or
arising directly or indirectly out of, in connection with or pursuant to any
claims by any Employees with respect to their employment with the Vendor.&nbsp; The
Purchaser shall indemnify and hold harmless the Vendor from and against all
Losses suffered or incurred by the Vendor as a result of or arising directly or
indirectly out of, in connection with or pursuant to an claims by any
Transferred Employees with respect to their employment with the Purchaser.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
No Employee shall be entitled to any rights under any of the provisions
of this Agreement.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Vendor shall not attempt in any way to discourage any of the
Employees from accepting any offer of employment to be made by the Purchaser
which is in compliance with this section 10.23<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380038003400350038003400310033000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> and shall not solicit the services of any of the Transferred
Employees while the Transferred Employee is employed by the Purchaser during the
year period following the Closing Date without the consent in writing of the
Purchaser, which consent may be unreasonably withheld.</p>
</blockquote>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<p align="justify"><a name="_Ref87715092">
<b>10.24</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Employee Plans</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser shall not assume any liability for accrued benefits under
any of the Employee Plans.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88480520">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser agrees that it will establish replacement plans (the "<b>Replacement</b>
<b>Plans</b>") for the Transferred Employees in respect of their employment by
the Purchaser from and after the Time of Closing.</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
For the purpose of determining the eligibility of a Transferred Employee
for membership or benefits under the Employee Plans and under the Replacement
Plans:</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
their period of employment shall include employment with both the Vendor
and the Purchaser and shall be deemed not to have been interrupted at the Time
of Closing; and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
their period of membership shall include membership in both the Employee
Plans and the Replacement Plans and shall be deemed not to have been interrupted
at the Time of Closing, provided that no Transferred Employee shall be entitled
to benefits under any disability plan sponsored by the Purchaser in respect of
any condition existing at or event occurring prior to the Time of Closing.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Transferred Employees shall begin to accrue benefits under the
Replacement Plans as of the Effective Time in respect of their employment by the
Purchaser.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
The Purchaser agrees to obtain the required approvals of the applicable
federal and provincial regulatory authorities in connection with the
establishment and registration of the Replacement Plans.</p>
</blockquote>
<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578254">
<b>10.25</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b>&nbsp;<u>Vendor's Access to Information</u></b></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p style="text-indent: 72; margin-left: 0in" align="justify">
<a name="_Toc88578255">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
Until reconciliation and payment of the Purchased Inventory Amount in full as
contemplated in this Agreement, the Purchaser shall provide weekly reports to
Robin Gray, or his replacement as designated by the Vendor, regarding the sale
of the Purchased Inventory through the Purchased Business.&nbsp; The form and
content of such reports shall be as agreed upon by the Purchaser and the Vendor
from time to time and full access shall be afforded by the Purchaser to Robin
Gray, or his replacement, to the sources of information relating to the subject
matter of the reports.&nbsp; The Vendor will employ Robin Gray, or his
replacement, for the purpose of reviewing the above-referenced reports and
reporting to the Vendor.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font> </a></p>
<font style="text-decoration: none">
<p class="Article1L1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">
<a name="_Toc88578256">Article 11<br>
</a><a name="_Ref88461541">CONDITIONS OF CLOSING</a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">
<p align="justify"><a name="_Ref87715620">
<b>11.1</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Conditions of Closing in Favour of the
Purchaser</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The sale and purchase of the Purchased
Assets is subject to the following terms and conditions for the exclusive
benefit of the Purchaser, to be performed or fulfilled at or prior to the Time
of Closing:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Representations and Warranties</u>.
The representations and warranties of the Vendor Group contained in this
Agreement shall be true and correct at the Time of Closing with the same force
and effect as if such representations and warranties were made at and as of such
time, and a certificate of an officer of each member of the Vendor Group, dated
the Closing Date, to that effect shall have been delivered to the Purchaser,
such certificate to be in form and substance satisfactory to the Purchaser,
acting reasonably;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Covenants</u>. All
of the terms, covenants and conditions of this Agreement to be complied with or
performed by each member of the Vendor Group at or before the Time of Closing
shall have been complied with or performed and a certificate of an officer of
each member of the Vendor Group, dated the Closing Date, to that effect shall
have been delivered to the Purchaser, such certificate to be in form and
substance satisfactory to the Purchaser, acting reasonably;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Regulatory Consents</u>.
There shall have been obtained from all appropriate Governmental Authorities
such licences, permits, consents, approvals, certificates, registrations and
authorizations as are required to be obtained by the Vendor to permit the change
of ownership of the Purchased Assets contemplated hereby, including without
limitation, the Competition Act Approval, as the foregoing may be amended from
time to time and any successor legislation thereto and those described in
Schedule 20, in each case in form and substance satisfactory to the Purchaser,
acting reasonably;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Contractual Consents</u>.
The Vendor shall have given or obtained the notices, consents and approvals
described in Schedule 21 (other than landlord consents to the assignment of the
Store Leases) in each case in form and substance satisfactory to the Purchaser,
acting reasonably;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Minimum Purchased Inventory</u>.&nbsp;
The ownership value of the Purchased Inventory as reflected in the WAR Report
dated December 4, 2004 shall be equal to or greater than $48,000,000, except as
a result of delays in the receipt of inventory;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" style="page-break-after: avoid" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Landlord Consents</u>.
The Purchaser shall have obtained:</p>
  <blockquote>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
written comfort, in a form and on terms and conditions acceptable to the
Purchaser in its sole and absolute discretion, from landlords representing at
least 80% of the Leased Stores in number, volume of sales and rent obligations,
that such landlords will provide their consent to the assignments by the Vendor
to the Purchaser of Store Leases representing&nbsp;80% of the Leased Stores in
number, volume of sales and rent obligations,&nbsp;such consents to be in forms and
on terms and conditions, acceptable to the Purchaser in its sole and absolute
discretion.&nbsp; Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, the
landlord consents shall fully describe the Store Leases and all amendments
thereto, and shall confirm the lease term, the amount of annual base or minimum
rent, additional rent and percentage rent payable thereunder, the amount of any
prepaid rent or security deposits paid to the landlord thereunder, whether the
Store Leases are currently in good standing and whether there are any disputes
between the Vendor and the landlord relating to the Store Leases; and</p>
<p class="Article1L4" align="justify">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="color: black">with respect to the Store Leases
representing no more than 20% of the Leased Stores in number, volume of sales
and rent obligations, the certificate of one of the officers of the Vendor<b>
</b>referred to in section 1.1(bbb)<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380038003000330035003400390039000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> confirming the lease term, the amount of the annual base or
minimum rent, additional rent and percentage rent payable thereunder, the amount
of any prepaid rent or security deposits paid to the landlord thereunder,
whether the Store Leases are currently in good standing and whether there are
any disputes between the Vendor and the landlord relating to the Stores Leases.</p>
  </blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87715120">(g)<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Sublease</u>. The
Vendor and the Purchaser shall have entered into a sublease agreement, in a form
satisfactory to the Purchaser and the Vendor (the "<b>Sublease</b>"), pursuant
to which the Purchaser will sublease the Head Office for a period of one year
and otherwise on the terms set forth in the Sublease</font></a><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Transitional Services Agreement</u>.
The Vendor shall have entered into the Transitional Services Agreement;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88561026">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Warehousing and Distribution</u>.
National Logistics Services shall have entered into a warehousing and
distribution agreement (the "<b>Warehousing and Distribution Agreement</b>")
with the Purchaser, at the same pricing as currently provided to the Vendor, for
a term of not less than four months and thereafter on a month to month basis for
up to an additional eight months at the Purchaser's option, in form and content
mutually satisfactory to the Purchaser and the Vendor;</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(j)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>No Action or Proceeding</u>.
No legal or regulatory action or proceeding shall be pending or threatened by
any Person to enjoin, restrict or prohibit the purchase and sale of the
Purchased Assets contemplated hereby;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(k)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Partnership Approval</u>.
The Vendor shall have provided evidence to the Purchaser of the approval of the
transactions contemplated in this Agreement by its partners in accordance with
the Limited Partnership Agreement and all applicable Laws;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(l)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Retail Sales Tax Certificates</u>.&nbsp;
The Vendor shall have delivered to the Purchaser certificates with respect to
the period ending up to September 30, 2004 issued by the Minister of Revenue of
Ontario under subsection 6(1) of the <i>Retail Sales Tax Act</i> (Ontario) and
from other applicable Governmental Authorities as required under any analogous
legislation in force in all other jurisdictions of Canada in which the Vendor
carries on or has carried on business;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(m)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>No Material Damage</u>.
No material damage by fire or other hazard to the whole or any material part of
the Purchased Assets shall have occurred from the date hereof to the Time of
Closing;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(n)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>No Material Adverse Change</u>.
There shall have been no Material Adverse Change since the date of the Financial
Statements;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(o)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Due Diligence</u>.
The results of Purchaser's due diligence investigations, including without
limitation, its business, financial and legal due diligence and Purchaser's
review of the Schedules, shall not reveal any facts or circumstances that would
render any representation or warranty of any member of the Vendor Group untrue
in a material respect;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(p)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Schedules.</u>&nbsp;
The contents of the Schedules to this Agreement shall be satisfactory to the
Purchaser, in its sole discretion; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(q)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Legal Opinion</u>.
The Vendor shall have delivered to the Purchaser a favourable opinion of counsel
to the Vendor and counsel to the other members of the Vendor Group in a form and
dealing with such matters as is satisfactory to the Purchaser and its counsel,
acting reasonably.</p>
</blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 125">If any of the conditions contained in
this section 11.1<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003600320030000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> shall not be performed or fulfilled at or prior to the Time
of Closing to the satisfaction of the Purchaser, acting reasonably, the
Purchaser may, by notice to the Vendor, terminate this Agreement and the
obligations of the Vendor and the Purchaser under this Agreement, other than the
obligations contained in sections 14.2<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003600330032000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> and 14.3<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003600330033000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]--> shall be terminated, provided that the Purchaser may also
bring an action pursuant to Article 13<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>

</xml><![endif]--> against the Vendor for damages suffered by the Purchaser
where the non-performance or non-fulfilment of the relevant condition is as a

<p align="justify"><a name="_Ref87715654">
<b>11.2</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Conditions of Closing in Favour of the Vendor</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The sale and purchase of the Purchased
Assets is subject to the following terms and conditions for the exclusive
benefit of the Vendor, to be performed or fulfilled at or prior to the Time of
Closing:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Representations and Warranties</u>.
The representations and warranties of the Purchaser contained in this Agreement

<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Covenants</u>. All
of the terms, covenants and conditions of this Agreement to be complied with or

dated the Closing Date, to that effect shall have been delivered to the Vendor,

reasonably;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Regulatory Consents</u>.
There shall have been obtained from all appropriate Governmental Authorities
such licences, permits, consents, approvals, certificates, registrations and
authorizations as are required to be obtained by the Purchaser to permit the
change of ownership of the Purchased Assets contemplated hereby, including those

Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Landlord Consents</u>.&nbsp;
The Purchaser shall have obtained landlord consents and estoppel certificates
(confirming the status of the applicable Store Lease, deposit (if any) and lease
term) from the top five landlords, who collectively represent at least 70% of
the Leased Stores;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Transitional Services Agreement</u>.
The Purchaser shall have entered into the Transitional Services Agreement; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Warehousing and Distribution</u>.
National Logistics Services shall have entered into a warehousing and
distribution agreement with the Purchaser on terms no less favourable than those
provided to the Vendor for a period of time of at least twelve months, in form
and content mutually satisfactory to the Purchaser and the Vendor;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Lease Guarantee.</u>&nbsp;
YM shall have delivered to the Vendor a guarantee, in a form satisfactory to the
Vendor and the Purchaser, guaranteeing the Purchaser's obligations under those
Store Leases to which the Vendor remains a party following the Closing Date;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(h)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>No Action or Proceeding</u>.
No legal or regulatory action or proceeding shall be pending or threatened by
any Person to enjoin, restrict or prohibit the purchase and sale of the
Purchased Assets contemplated hereby; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u>Schedules</u>.&nbsp;
The contents of the Schedules to this Agreement shall be satisfactory to the
Vendor, in its sole discretion. </p>
</blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 125">If any of the conditions contained in
this section 11.2<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003600350034000000</w:data>

</font></font></font></font>
</font>
<font style="text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">
<a name="_Toc88578259">Article 12<br>
CLOSING DATE AND TRANSFER OR POSSESSION</a></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<p align="justify"><a name="_Toc88578260">
<b>12.1</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="text-decoration: underline"><u><b>Transfer</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">Subject to compliance with the terms and
conditions hereof, the transfer of possession of the Purchased Assets shall be
deemed to take effect at the Effective Time.</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578261">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<b>12.2</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><u><b>Place of Closing</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify">The closing shall take place at the Time
of Closing at the offices of Gowling Lafleur Henderson LLP, counsel for the
Purchaser, Suite 5800, Scotia Plaza, 40 King Street West, Toronto, Ontario, M5H
3Z7.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref88463044">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>12.3</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Further Assurances</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">From time to time subsequent to the
Closing Date, each Party covenants and agrees that it will at all times after
the Closing Date, at the expense of the requesting party, promptly execute and
deliver all such documents, including, without limitation, all such additional
conveyances, transfers, consents and other assurances and do all such other acts
and things as the other Party, acting reasonably, may from time to time request
be executed or done in order to better evidence or perfect or effectuate any
provision of this Agreement or of any agreement or other document executed
pursuant to this Agreement or any of the respective obligations intended to be
created hereby or thereby.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87715698">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>12.4</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Waiver of Bulk Sales Act</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The Purchaser and the Vendor waive
compliance by the Vendor of the provisions of the <i>Bulk Sales Act </i>
(Ontario) and any analogous legislation in force in all other jurisdictions of
Canada in which the Vendor carries on business.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578264">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>12.5</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><u><b>Risk of Loss</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
From the Execution Date up to the Effective Time, the Purchased Assets
shall be and remain at the risk of the Vendor and the Purchased Trademarks shall
be and remain at the risk of the Trademark Vendor.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
If, prior to the Time of Closing, all or any part of the Purchased Assets
are destroyed or damaged by fire or any other casualty or shall be appropriated,
expropriated or seized by any Governmental Authority, unless the Purchaser
terminates its obligations under this Agreement as contemplated by section 11.1<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003600320030000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->, the Purchaser shall complete the purchase without reduction
of the Purchase Price, provided that all proceeds of insurance payable to the
Vendor (including insurance proceeds for business interruption until such time
as the damaged or destroyed Leased Store is rebuilt and/or refurbished) or
compensation for expropriation or seizure shall be paid to the Purchaser at the
Time of Closing and all right and claim of the Vendor to any such amounts not
paid by the Closing Date shall be assigned at the Time of Closing to the
Purchaser.</p>
</blockquote>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="Article1L1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">
<a name="_Ref87746506">Article 13<br>
INDEMNIFICATION</a></p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578266">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.1</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Indemnification by the Vendor</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">Each member of the Vendor Group jointly
and severally agrees to indemnify and save harmless the Purchaser from all
Losses suffered or incurred by the Purchaser as a result of or arising directly
or indirectly out of or in connection with:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any breach by any of the Vendor Group, or any inaccuracy, of any
representation or warranty of a member of the Vendor Group contained in this
Agreement or in any agreement, certificate or other document delivered pursuant
hereto;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any breach or non-performance by a member of the Vendor Group of any
covenant to be performed by one or more of them which is contained in this
Agreement or in any agreement, certificate or other document delivered pursuant
hereto;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the use of the Purchased Trademarks up to the Effective Time;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88483930">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any commission or other remuneration payable or alleged to be payable to
any broker, agent or other intermediary who purports to act or have acted for or
on behalf of the Vendor;</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87946048">(e)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
notwithstanding section 12.4<!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <w:data>08D0C9EA79F9BACE118C8200AA004BA90B02000000080000000D0000005F00520065006600380037003700310035003600390038000000</w:data>
</xml><![endif]-->, any non-compliance with the <i>Bulk Sales Act</i> (Ontario)
or any analogous legislation in force in any other jurisdiction of Canada in
which the Vendor carries on business; and</a></p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref87946062">(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the Excluded Liabilities.</a></p>
</blockquote>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578267">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.2</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Indemnification by the Purchaser</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">The Purchaser agrees to indemnify and
save harmless the Vendor and the Trademark Vendor from all Losses suffered or
incurred by the Vendor as a result of or arising directly or indirectly out of
or in connection with:</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any breach by the Purchaser of or any inaccuracy of any representation or
warranty contained in this Agreement or in any agreement, instrument,
certificate or other document delivered pursuant hereto;</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
any breach or non-performance by the Purchaser of any covenant to be
performed by it which is contained in this Agreement or in any agreement,
certificate or other document delivered pursuant hereto.</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify"><a name="_Ref88889150">(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the operations of the Purchased Business after the Time of Closing
including, without limitation, any failure by the Purchaser to pay, satisfy,
discharge, perform or fulfil any of the Assumed Liabilities.</a></p>
</blockquote>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Ref87714684">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.3</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Notice of Claim</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">In the event that a Party (the "<b>Indemnified
Party</b>") shall become aware of any claim, proceeding or other matter (a "<b>Claim</b>")
in respect of which the other Party (the "<b>Indemnifying Party</b>") agreed to
indemnify the Indemnified Party pursuant to this Agreement, the Indemnified
Party shall promptly give written notice thereof to the Indemnifying Party. Such
notice shall specify whether the Claim arises as a result of a claim by a Person
against the Indemnified Party (a "<b>Third Party Claim</b>") or whether the
Claim does not so arise (a "<b>Direct</b> <b>Claim</b>"), and shall also specify
with reasonable particularity (to the extent that the information is available):</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(a)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the factual basis for the Claim; and</p>
<p class="Article1L3" align="justify">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
the amount of the Claim, if known.</p>
</blockquote>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">If, through the fault of the Indemnified
Party, the Indemnifying Party does not receive notice of any Claim in time
effectively to contest the determination of any liability susceptible of being
contested, the Indemnifying Party shall be entitled to set off against the
amount claimed by the Indemnified Party the amount of any Losses incurred by the
Indemnifying Party resulting from the Indemnified Party's failure to give such
notice on a timely basis.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578269">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.4</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Direct Claims</b></u></font></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">With respect to any Direct Claim,
following receipt of notice from the Indemnified Party of the Claim, the
Indemnifying Party shall have 60 days to make such investigation of the Claim as
is considered necessary or desirable. For the purpose of such investigation, the
Indemnified Party shall make available to the Indemnifying Party the information
relied upon by the Indemnified Party to substantiate the Claim, together with
all such other information as the Indemnifying Party may reasonably request. If
both Parties agree at or prior to the expiration of such 60-day period (or any
mutually agreed upon extension thereof) to the validity and amount of such
Claim, the Indemnifying Party shall immediately pay to the Indemnified Party the
full agreed upon amount of the Claim, failing which the matter shall be
determined by a court of competent jurisdiction.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578270">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.5</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Third Party Claims</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">With respect to any Third Party Claim,
the Indemnifying Party shall have the right, at its expense, to participate in
or assume control of the negotiation, settlement or defence of the Claim and, in
such event, the Indemnifying Party shall reimburse the Indemnified Party for all
the Indemnified Party's out-of-pocket expenses as a result of such participation
or assumption. If the Indemnifying Party elects to assume such control, the
Indemnified Party shall have the right to participate in the negotiation,
settlement or defence of such Third Party Claim and to retain counsel to act on
its behalf, provided that the fees and disbursements of such counsel shall be
paid by the Indemnified Party unless the Indemnifying Party consents to the
retention of such counsel or unless the named parties to any action or
proceeding include both the Indemnifying Party and the Indemnified Party and a
representation of both the Indemnifying Party and the Indemnified Party by the
same counsel would be inappropriate due to the actual or potential differing
interests between them (such as the availability of different defences). If the
Indemnifying Party, having elected to assume such control, thereafter fails to
defend the Third Party Claim within a reasonable time, the Indemnified Party
shall be entitled to assume such control and the Indemnifying Party shall be
bound by the results obtained by the Indemnified Party with respect to such
Third Party Claim. If any Third Party Claim is of a nature such that the
Indemnified Party is required by applicable law to make a payment to any Person
(a "<b>Third</b> <b>Party</b>") with respect to the Third Party Claim before the
completion of settlement negotiations or related legal proceedings, the
Indemnified Party may make such payment and the Indemnifying Party shall,
forthwith after demand by the Indemnified Party, reimburse the Indemnified Party
for such payment If the amount of any liability of the Indemnified Party under
the Third Party Claim in respect of which such a payment was made, as finally
determined, is less than the amount which was paid by the Indemnifying Party to
the Indemnified Party, the Indemnified Party shall, forthwith after receipt of
the difference from the Third Party, pay the amount of such difference to the
Indemnifying Party.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578271">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.6</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<u><b>Settlement of Third Party Claims</b></u></font></a></p>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">If the Indemnifying Party fails to
assume control of the defence of any Third Party Claim, the Indemnified Party
shall have the exclusive right to contest, settle or pay the amount claimed.
Whether or not the Indemnifying Party assumes control of the negotiation,
settlement or defence of any Third Party Claim, the Indemnifying Party shall not
settle any Third Party Claim without the written consent of the Indemnified
Party, which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld or delayed; provided,
however, that the liability of the Indemnifying Party shall be limited to the
proposed settlement amount if any such consent is not obtained for any reason.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"></font><a name="_Toc88578272">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<b>13.7</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline">
<u><b>Co-operation</b></u></font></font></a></p>
</font></font></font></font></font></font></font></font>
</font></font></font></font></font></font>
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">
<font style="color: black; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none; color:black">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; color:black">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; color:black">
<font style="color: black; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal; text-decoration:none">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; color: black">The Indemnified Party and the
Indemnifying Party shall cooperate fully with each other with respect to Third
Party Claims, and shall keep each other fully advised with respect thereto
(including supplying copies of all relevant documentation promptly as it becomes
available).</font></font></font></font></font></font></p>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:none">

<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font>
<font style="text-decoration: underline; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman"></font>
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">

<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-size:12.0pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman; text-decoration:underline"></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal; text-decoration: none">

<b>14.4</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">

<p align="justify"><b>14.5</b><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Force Majeure Event </b></u></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-autospace: none; margin-bottom: .0001pt; text-indent:72" align="justify">Any
failure or omission by a party in the performance of any obligation under this
Agreement arising from any cause or causes beyond the control of such party
shall be suspended to the extent and for the period that performance is
prevented (to a maximum of three Business Days in respect of obligations for the
payment of money) and during such suspension shall not be deemed a breach of
this Agreement or create any liability, if the same arises from any cause or
causes beyond the control of such party, including, but not limited to, the
following, which for purposes of this Agreement shall be regarded as beyond the
control of each of the parties hereto: acts of God, fire, storm, flood,
earthquake, governmental regulation or direction, acts of a public enemy, war,
rebellion, insurrection, riot, terrorism, invasion, strike or lockout; provided
that the Party relying on the provisions of this section shall forthwith give to
the others notice of such suspension, the reasons therefor and the expected
duration thereof.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p align="justify"><b>14.6</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<u><b>Counterparts and Facsimile</b></u></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size: 12.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="BodyText1" align="justify" style="text-indent: 72">This Agreement may be executed in
counterparts, each of which shall constitute an original and all of which taken
together shall constitute one and the same instrument. Delivery of this
Agreement by facsimile shall be satisfactory and valid execution and delivery of
this Agreement.</p>
<p class="BodyText1"><b>IN WITNESS WHEREOF</b>
this Agreement has been executed by the Parties on the date first written above.</p>
