<p class="OHHpara2" style="text-indent: -67.5pt" align="right"><i>Exhibit 2.2<br>
&nbsp;</i></p>
<p class="OHHpara2" style="text-indent: -67.5pt" align="left">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b>THIS
ASSET PURCHASE AMENDING AGREEMENT</b> is made
as of
December 10, 2004</p>
<p class="Boldsubtitle"><b>BETWEEN: </b> </p>
<blockquote>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left">
<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 6295215 CANADA INC.</b>,
a corporation governed by the laws of
Canada,</p>
</blockquote>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left">
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
(the <b>&quot;Purchaser&quot;</b>)</p>
<p class="OHHCentre" align="left">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; - and -</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left; line-height: normal">
<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; BLUENOTES LIMITED PARTNERSHIP, </b>
a limited partnership formed under the laws of the Province
of Ontario,</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left">
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
(the <b>&quot;Vendor&quot;</b>)</p>
<p class="OHHCentre">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; - and -</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left; line-height: normal">
<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; RETAIL LICENSING COMPANY</b>, a
corporation existing under the laws of the State of Nevada,</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left">
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
(the <b>&quot;Trademark Vendor&quot;</b>)</p>
<p class="Centre">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; - and -</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left; line-height: normal">
<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; AMERICAN EAGLE OUTFITTERS CANADA CORPORATION,</b>
an unlimited liability company existing under the laws of the Province of Nova
Scotia,</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (<b>&quot;American
Eagle </b><b>Canada&quot;</b>)</p>
<p class="Centre">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; - and -</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left; line-height: normal">
<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3049463 NOVA SCOTIA ULC</b>, an
unlimited liability company existing under the laws of the Province of Nova
Scotia,</p>
<p class="OHHpara2" align="left" style="text-align: left">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (<b>&quot;GP&quot;</b>)</p>
<p class="recitals" style="page-break-after: avoid"><b>
RECITALS</b>:</p>
<p class="ClosingL2" style="line-height: normal">A.<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font size="3">The Parties are all party to an asset purchase agreement dated November
22, 2004 (the <b>&quot;Purchase Agreement&quot;</b>).</font></p>
<p class="ClosingL2" style="line-height: normal">B.</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size:7.0pt"><font size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;The Purchase Agreement contemplates the purchase and sale of the
Purchased Assets and the Purchased Trademarks and the assumption of the Assumed
Liabilities on December 5, 2004 or such other date as the Vendor and Purchaser
may agree in writing.</font></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="ClosingL2" align="left" style="text-align: left; line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt">
C.</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman"><font size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By a letter agreement dated December 3, 2004, the Parties agreed to
extend the Closing Date to December 10, 2004 (the &quot;<b>Letter Agreement</b>&quot;).<br>
<br>
</font>
</font>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">D.</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman"><font size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Parties desire to make certain amendments to the Purchase Agreement.</font></p>
</font>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara"><b>THEREFORE</b>,
the Parties agree as follows:</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">
ARTICLE 1&nbsp;<br>
<br>
INTERPRETATION<br>
&nbsp;</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman"></p>
<p class="OHHpara"><b>1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Asset Purchase Amending Agreement</b></p>
<p class="OHHpara">This asset purchase amending agreement supersedes and
replaces the Letter Agreement.</p>
<p class="OHHpara"><b>1.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Defined Terms.</b></p>
<p class="OHHpara">All defined terms used herein shall have the meanings
ascribed to such terms in the Purchase Agreement, unless otherwise defined
herein.<br>
&nbsp;</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL1" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in" align="center">ARTICLE 2&nbsp;</p>
<p class="ArticleL1" align="center">ASSET PURCHASE AMENDING AGREEMENT</p>
<p class="ArticleL2">2.1</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size:7.0pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight:700" size="3">Effective Closing Time</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">Section 1 of the Purchase
Agreement is hereby amended as follows:</p>
<p class="ArticleL4">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (i)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
to add as a new definition the following immediately above subsection
1.1(v):<br>
<br>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
&quot;(v1)<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &quot;Effective Closing Time&quot;</b> means
12:01 a.m. on December 5, 2004.&quot;</p>
<p class="ArticleL4">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (ii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
to add in subsection 1.1(jj) at the end of the definition of <b>&quot;Final
Amount&quot;</b>, the following:</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL4" style="text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &quot;and means an
amount equal to the aggregate of the lesser of (a) the Vendor's cost of the
buttons and (b) 50% of the Average Retail Value of the buttons sold by the
Purchaser in the week ending April 2, 2005, per unit of button which forms part
of the Remaining Inventory.&quot;</p>
<p class="ArticleL4">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (iii)</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
to add in subsection 1.1(eeee) <b>&quot;Remaining Inventory&quot;</b> after the
words Purchased Inventory, the following:<br>
<br>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
&nbsp;&quot;including all units of buttons&quot;.&nbsp; </p>
<p class="ArticleL4">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; All references in the
Purchase Agreement to <b>&quot;Inventory In-Transit&quot;</b> and <b>&quot;Inventory On Hand&quot;</b>
shall be read to include all units of buttons.</p>
</font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL4" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 1.0in">
&nbsp;</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL2">2.2</font><font style="font-size: 14.0pt; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman; font-weight:700" size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Closing Date</p>
</font>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">
The reference to &quot;December 5, 2004&quot; is deleted from the
definition of &quot;Closing Date&quot; in the Purchase Agreement and replaced with one
business day following the date on which all of the conditions for closing in
Article 11 have been satisfied or waived. The
definitions of &quot;Working Capital Assets&quot; and &quot;Working Capital Liabilities&quot; are
amended to delete all references to &quot;Closing Date&quot; and replace them with
references to &quot;Effective Closing Time&quot;.<b> </b>The definitions of&nbsp; &quot;Petty Cash&quot;
and &quot;Store Floats&quot; are amended to delete all references to &quot;Effective Time&quot; and
replace them with reference to &quot;Effective Closing Time&quot;. </p>
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal"><b>2.3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Closing Condition</b></p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">For purposes
of subsection 11.1(f)(i), the Purchaser agrees that: (a) delivery to the
Purchaser of a fully executed landlord assignment in respect of each Store
Lease, in a form agreed upon by the Vendor and the Purchaser, shall constitute
one of the forms of written comfort acceptable to the Purchaser; and (b) the
reference to volume of sales therein shall be with reference to volume of sales
in the relevant Leased Store for the 12 month period ended November 28, 2004.</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:700; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL1" align="center">ARTICLE 3</p>
<p class="ArticleL1" align="center">EFFECTIVE DATE CLOSING</p>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL2" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in">
<b>
<a name="_Toc12179409">3.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Effective Date</a></b></font><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-family:Times New Roman; "><b>
</b>
</font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">
Notwithstanding anything in the Purchase Agreement to the contrary, it is the
intention of the Parties that the economic effect of the purchase and sale of
the Purchased Assets and the Purchased Trademarks and the assumption of the
Assumed Liabilities pursuant to the Purchase Agreement shall be as of the
Effective Closing Time.&nbsp; In order to give effect to the foregoing, the Vendor
shall pay to the Purchaser or the Purchaser shall pay to the Vendor the amounts
contemplated in Section 2.2 at the time(s) and in accordance with the provisions
of such Section.&nbsp; Such payment shall be treated as a reduction (increase) in the
Purchased Asset Amount if paid by the Vendor (Purchaser).</p>
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal"><b>3.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Determination of Net Cash Receipts </b></p>
<p style="text-indent: -.5in; line-height: normal; margin-left: 1.0in">
(a)<b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </b></font><b>
<font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp; </font> </b><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">At Closing, the Vendor shall credit in
favour of the Purchaser against the Closing Date Amount, 50% of the Net Sales
Proceeds for sales at all of the Leased Stores other than the Excluded Leased
Store, plus 25% of the Net Sales Proceeds for sales at the Excluded Leased
Store, in respect of the period from December 5 to and including December 11,
2004. The Parties shall perform a reconciliation of the actual amount of the Net
Sales Proceeds and the corresponding amount credited against the Closing Date
Amount pursuant to this subsection 3.2(a), and any difference shall be adjusted
between the Parties following Closing.</p>
<p style="text-indent: -.5in; line-height: normal; margin-left: 1.0in">
(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Vendor shall account to the Purchaser for cash
receipts by the Vendor from sales to customers (&quot;Cash Receipts&quot;) during the
period from and including December 12, 2004 to the Effective Time (the &quot;Intervening Period&quot;) less cash disbursements by the Vendor and the Parent made
in the ordinary course in connection with the operation of the Purchased
Business (&quot;Cash Disbursements&quot;) during the Intervening Period.
</font><font style="font-weight: normal">
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">
</p>
<p style="text-indent: -.5in; line-height: normal; margin-left: 1.0in">
(a)</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3"><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Vendor shall notify the Purchaser of its determination of Cash Receipts and Cash
Disbursements no later than five (5)</font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">Business Days after the
Closing Date.&nbsp; The Purchaser shall have three (3) Business Days following
receipt of such notice to </font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">review the Vendor</font><font style="font-weight: normal">'</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">s
determination.&nbsp; The Purchase shall have access to all documents in the
possession or under the control </font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">of the Vendor or any of
its affiliates, reasonably required for such review. If no written objection is
made by the Purchaser </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">within the aforesaid time
period, the amounts determined by the Vendor shall be final and binding upon the
Parties.</p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">
<font style="font-weight: normal">
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">(b)</font></font><font style="font-size: 14.0pt; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman"><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
In the event that the Purchaser gives to the Vendor a written notice of
objection within such three (3) Business Day period,
</font>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">
<font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">the Purchaser and the
Vendor shall attempt in good faith to resolve the matters in dispute. If the
matters in dispute are not </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">resolved within five (5)&nbsp; Business Days after the
delivery of the notice of dispute, the matters in dispute not resolved will be
</font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">submitted to the Arbitrator. The Arbitrator shall be instructed by the Vendor
and the Purchaser to make a determination as </font>
<font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">to all remaining matters in dispute
within ten (10)&nbsp; Business Days of the submission of same. The Arbitrator shall
be further </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">instructed by the Vendor and the Purchaser to choose between the
positions adopted by the Vendor and the Purchaser.&nbsp; The determinations of the
Arbitrator shall be final and binding upon the Parties. Each of the Vendor and
the Purchaser, shall pay 50% of the fees and expenses of the Arbitrator in
connection with the performance of the duties imposed upon it under this Section&nbsp;10.2.</font></font></font><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman"><font lang="EN-CA"><font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-family:Times New Roman"><blockquote>
<p>(c)</font></font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3"><font lang="EN-CA">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<font lang="EN-CA">Th</font></font><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7.0pt; font-family: Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 14.0pt; font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman"><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal"><font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">e
amount by which Cash Receipts exceeds (or is exceeded by) Cash Disbursements
shall by paid by the Vendor
</font>
</font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman" size="3">
<font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">(Purchaser) within ten
(10) Business Days after the Closing Date provided that if the Purchaser has
given written </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">notice of an objection to
the Vendor</font><font style="font-weight: normal">'</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">s determination of Cash Receipts and Cash Disbursements, the amount
to be </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">paid by the Vendor or
Purchaser within such ten (10) Business Day period shall be the amount which is
not in </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">dispute and the remainder
will be paid forthwith following final determination of the dispute in
accordance with </font><font style="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">subsection (c).</p>
</blockquote>
</font>
</font>
</font></font><font lang="EN-CA">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:700">
<p class="ArticleL2" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in">3.3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Remittances</p>
</font></font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">
<font style="font-style:normal; font-variant:normal; font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">The Purchaser covenants and
agrees to remit on a timely basis all amounts received by it as part of the Cash
Receipts which are required to be remitted on account of payroll Taxes, Sales
Taxes and GST with respect to the Intervening Period.</p>

<font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: 700">
<p class="ArticleL1" align="center">ARTICLE 5</p>
<p class="ArticleL1" align="center">GENERAL</p>
</font></font><font lang="EN-CA">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="ArticleL2" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in">
5.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Full Force and Effect</p>
</font></font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">The Purchase
Agreement as amended by this asset purchase amending agreement shall remain in
full force and effect., and all references to the Agreement shall be read to
include this asset purchase amending agreement.</p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
<font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: 700">
<p class="ArticleL2" style="text-indent: 0in; margin-left: 0in">
5.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Counterparts</p>
</font></font><font lang="EN-CA" style="font-weight: normal">
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">
<p class="OHHpara" style="line-height: normal">This Agreement
may be executed in any number of counterparts, by facsimile signature or
otherwise, each of which when so executed shall be deemed to be an original, and
all such counterparts taken together shall be deemed to constitute one
agreement, effective as of the date first indicated above.</p>
</font></font>
<font style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-family: Times New Roman">

This agreement shall be governed
by and interpreted in accordance with the law of the Province of Ontario, and
the federal law of Canada applicable therein.</p>
</font></font>

<body>

<h5 style="text-align: right"><font style="text-decoration: none">

<B><FONT SIZE=2 face="Times New Roman">

EXHIBIT 99.1</FONT></B></font></h5>

<h5 align="center">&nbsp;</h5>

<h5 align="center"><font face="GillSans" size="3"><u>NEWS RELEASE</u></font><b><font style="font-family: GillSans">&nbsp;</font></b></h5>
<h3 align="center" style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">
<font style="font-size: 16pt; " face="Garamond">AMERICAN EAGLE</font></h3>
<h3 align="center" style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">
<font style="font-size: 16pt; " face="Garamond">OUTFITTERS</font><font style="font-size: 16.0pt; font-family: Garamond">&nbsp;</font></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align: center"><b>
<font style="font-size: 16.0pt; font-family: Garamond; color: black">Completes
the Sale</font><font style="font-size: 16.0pt; font-family: Garamond; color: black">
of Bluenotes</font></b><font style="font-family: GillSans; color: blue">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 115%">
<font size="2" style="line-height: 115%; color: black">Warrendale, PA,
December 21, 2004 - American Eagle Outfitters, Inc. (NASDAQ: AEOS) today
announced that the Company completed the disposition of its Bluenotes retail
apparel business.&nbsp; The transaction is effective as of December 5, 2004. &nbsp;&nbsp;</font></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 115%; margin-right: 6.3pt">
<font style="line-height: 115%"><font size="2">American Eagle Outfitters
(NASDAQ: AEOS) is a leading lifestyle retailer that designs, markets, and sells
its own brand of relaxed, casual clothing for 15 to 25 year olds, providing
high-quality merchandise at affordable prices.&nbsp; AE's collection includes modern
basics like jeans, cargo pants, and graphic Ts as well as a stylish assortment
of cool accessories, outerwear and footwear. AE's Canadian subsidiary,
Bluenotes/Thriftys, offers a more urban/suburban, denim-driven collection for 12
to 22 year olds.&nbsp; American Eagle Outfitters currently operates 780 AE stores in
49 states, the District of Columbia and Puerto Rico, 69 AE stores in Canada, and
109 Bluenotes/Thriftys stores in Canada. AE also operates via its Web business,
www.ae.com, which offers additional sizes and styles of favorite AE merchandise.</font></font></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 115%; margin-right: 6.3pt">
<font face="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><b>Company Contacts</b>:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>
<br>
Laura Weil<br>
Judy Meehan<br>
724-776-4857</font></p>

</body>

</html>

<p align="right" style="margin-bottom: 0">
<b><font size="2">EXHIBIT 99.2</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin-bottom: 0">
<FONT size=2><B>
UNAUDITED PRO FORMA CONSOLIDATED</B></FONT></p>
<p align="center" style="margin-top: 0">
<FONT size=2><B>
FINANCIAL STATEMENTS OF AMERICAN EAGLE OUTFITTERS, INC.<BR>
&nbsp;</B></FONT></p>
<p align="justify" style="margin-top: 0"><font size="2">The following unaudited
pro forma condensed consolidated financial information of American Eagle
Outfitters, Inc. (the &quot;Company&quot;) gives effect to the disposition of the
Bluenotes business by the Company to a private company controlled by Mr. Michael
Gold, owner of YM Inc., (Sales), a prominent Canadian retailer (the
&quot;Purchaser&quot;).&nbsp; The accompanying unaudited pro forma condensed consolidated
statements of operations for the nine month period ended October 30, 2004 and
for the year ended January 31, 2004 give effect to the disposition as if it had
occurred on February 2, 2003.&nbsp; The unaudited pro forma condensed
consolidated balance sheet as of October 30, 2004 reflects the disposition as if
it had occurred on that date.&nbsp; All pro forma adjustments are described in
the notes to the unaudited condensed consolidated financial statements and are
based upon available information and certain assumptions that the Company
believes are reasonable under the circumstances.</font></p>
<p align="justify" style="margin-top: 0"><font size="2">This pro forma
information is based on and should be read in conjunction with the financial
statements and notes thereto included in the Company's Annual Report on Form
10-K for the year ended January 31, 2004 and the Company's Quarterly Report on
Form 10-Q for the period ended October 30, 2004.&nbsp; The unaudited pro forma
financial information is for illustrative purposes only and is not necessarily
indicative of the financial position or results of operations that would have
occurred if the transaction has taken place on the dates indicated and is not
necessarily indicative of future financial position or results of operations.</font></p>

<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">Pro Forma Adjustments</B></P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(A)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect  cash proceeds from the sale
of $12.3 million, partially offset by $0.3
million of working capital adjustments.&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(B)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect assets sold to
the Purchaser.</P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(C)&nbsp; Adjustment primarily to record
$9.4 million in accounts receivable which represents proceeds from
the sale.&nbsp; This amount is estimated based
upon expected future inventory sales by the purchaser through April 2, 2005, in accordance with the
purchase agreement.</P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(D)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect an increase
in the income tax benefit attributed to the net operating loss
caused by the pro forma loss on the transaction.&nbsp; No valuation allowance
has been recorded against this amount as the Company anticipates that future
taxable income in Canada will be sufficient to utilize the full amount of the
deferred tax asset.&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(E)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect accruals
of $3.8 million in estimated direct expenses, including various personnel
expenses, real estate/legal fees and appropriate reserves and taxes for the transaction.&nbsp; Note that the accruals
of estimated direct expenses and appropriate reserves were not considered in preparation of the pro forma
income statements as these amounts were deemed nonrecurring in nature.</P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(F)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect the reversal
of accumulated other comprehensive income related to foreign currency
translation.</P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(G)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect the pro
forma loss resulting from the sale, net of tax benefit.</P>
<P align=left style="margin-top: 0">(H)&nbsp; Adjustment to reflect the elimination of
revenue, expenses and related taxes attributed to Bluenotes.</P>
